import Tip from "../../Tip.svelte";

export let fw: "pt" | "tf"
&amp;lt;/script>

# Auto Classes

In many cases, the architecture you want to use can be guessed from the name or the path of the pretrained model you
are supplying to the `from_pretrained()` method. AutoClasses are here to do this job for you so that you
automatically retrieve the relevant model given the name/path to the pretrained weights/config/vocabulary.

Instantiating one of [AutoConfig](model_doc/auto.html#transformers.AutoConfig), [AutoModel](model_doc/auto.html#transformers.AutoModel), and
[AutoTokenizer](model_doc/auto.html#transformers.AutoTokenizer) will directly create a class of the relevant architecture. For instance


```python
model = AutoModel.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
```

will create a model that is an instance of [BertModel](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertModel).

There is one class of `AutoModel` for each task, and for each backend (PyTorch or TensorFlow).


## AutoConfig

<a id='transformers.AutoConfig'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoConfig**()


This is a generic configuration class that will be instantiated as one of the configuration classes of the library
when created with the [from_pretrained()](model_doc/auto.html#transformers.AutoConfig.from_pretrained) class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.AutoConfig.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(pretrained_model_name_or_path, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the configuration classes of the library from a pretrained model configuration.

The configuration class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object
that is loaded, or when it's missing, by falling back to using pattern matching on
`pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) (ALBERT model)
- **bart** -- [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) (BART model)
- **beit** -- [BeitConfig](model_doc/beit.html#transformers.BeitConfig) (BeiT model)
- **bert** -- [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) (BERT model)
- **bert-generation** -- [BertGenerationConfig](model_doc/bertgeneration.html#transformers.BertGenerationConfig) (Bert Generation model)
- **big_bird** -- [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) (BigBird model)
- **bigbird_pegasus** -- [BigBirdPegasusConfig](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusConfig) (BigBirdPegasus model)
- **blenderbot** -- [BlenderbotConfig](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.BlenderbotConfig) (Blenderbot model)
- **blenderbot-small** -- [BlenderbotSmallConfig](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.BlenderbotSmallConfig) (BlenderbotSmall model)
- **camembert** -- [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) (CamemBERT model)
- **canine** -- [CanineConfig](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineConfig) (Canine model)
- **clip** -- [CLIPConfig](model_doc/clip.html#transformers.CLIPConfig) (CLIP model)
- **convbert** -- [ConvBertConfig](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertConfig) (ConvBERT model)
- **ctrl** -- [CTRLConfig](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLConfig) (CTRL model)
- **deberta** -- [DebertaConfig](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaConfig) (DeBERTa model)
- **deberta-v2** -- [DebertaV2Config](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Config) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
- **deit** -- [DeiTConfig](model_doc/deit.html#transformers.DeiTConfig) (DeiT model)
- **detr** -- [DetrConfig](model_doc/detr.html#transformers.DetrConfig) (DETR model)
- **distilbert** -- [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) (DistilBERT model)
- **dpr** -- [DPRConfig](model_doc/dpr.html#transformers.DPRConfig) (DPR model)
- **electra** -- [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) (ELECTRA model)
- **encoder-decoder** -- [EncoderDecoderConfig](model_doc/encoderdecoder.html#transformers.EncoderDecoderConfig) (Encoder decoder model)
- **flaubert** -- [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) (FlauBERT model)
- **fnet** -- [FNetConfig](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetConfig) (FNet model)
- **fsmt** -- [FSMTConfig](model_doc/fsmt.html#transformers.FSMTConfig) (FairSeq Machine-Translation model)
- **funnel** -- [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **gpt2** -- [GPT2Config](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Config) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
- **gpt_neo** -- [GPTNeoConfig](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.GPTNeoConfig) (GPT Neo model)
- **gptj** -- [GPTJConfig](model_doc/gptj.html#transformers.GPTJConfig) (GPT-J model)
- **hubert** -- [HubertConfig](model_doc/hubert.html#transformers.HubertConfig) (Hubert model)
- **ibert** -- [IBertConfig](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertConfig) (I-BERT model)
- **layoutlm** -- [LayoutLMConfig](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMConfig) (LayoutLM model)
- **layoutlmv2** -- [LayoutLMv2Config](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2Config) (LayoutLMv2 model)
- **led** -- [LEDConfig](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDConfig) (LED model)
- **longformer** -- [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) (Longformer model)
- **luke** -- [LukeConfig](model_doc/luke.html#transformers.LukeConfig) (LUKE model)
- **lxmert** -- [LxmertConfig](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertConfig) (LXMERT model)
- **m2m_100** -- [M2M100Config](model_doc/m2m_100.html#transformers.M2M100Config) (M2M100 model)
- **marian** -- [MarianConfig](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianConfig) (Marian model)
- **mbart** -- [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) (mBART model)
- **megatron-bert** -- [MegatronBertConfig](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertConfig) (MegatronBert model)
- **mobilebert** -- [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) (MPNet model)
- **mt5** -- [MT5Config](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.MT5Config) (mT5 model)
- **openai-gpt** -- [OpenAIGPTConfig](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTConfig) (OpenAI GPT model)
- **pegasus** -- [PegasusConfig](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusConfig) (Pegasus model)
- **prophetnet** -- [ProphetNetConfig](model_doc/prophetnet.html#transformers.ProphetNetConfig) (ProphetNet model)
- **rag** -- [RagConfig](model_doc/rag.html#transformers.RagConfig) (RAG model)
- **reformer** -- [ReformerConfig](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerConfig) (Reformer model)
- **rembert** -- [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) (RemBERT model)
- **retribert** -- [RetriBertConfig](model_doc/retribert.html#transformers.RetriBertConfig) (RetriBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) (RoFormer model)
- **speech-encoder-decoder** -- [SpeechEncoderDecoderConfig](model_doc/speechencoderdecoder.html#transformers.SpeechEncoderDecoderConfig) (Speech Encoder decoder model)
- **speech_to_text** -- [Speech2TextConfig](model_doc/speech_to_text.html#transformers.Speech2TextConfig) (Speech2Text model)
- **speech_to_text_2** -- [Speech2Text2Config](model_doc/speech_to_text_2.html#transformers.Speech2Text2Config) (Speech2Text2 model)
- **splinter** -- [SplinterConfig](model_doc/splinter.html#transformers.SplinterConfig) (Splinter model)
- **squeezebert** -- [SqueezeBertConfig](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertConfig) (SqueezeBERT model)
- **t5** -- [T5Config](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Config) (T5 model)
- **tapas** -- [TapasConfig](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasConfig) (TAPAS model)
- **transfo-xl** -- [TransfoXLConfig](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLConfig) (Transformer-XL model)
- **visual_bert** -- [VisualBertConfig](model_doc/visual_bert.html#transformers.VisualBertConfig) (VisualBert model)
- **vit** -- [ViTConfig](model_doc/vit.html#transformers.ViTConfig) (ViT model)
- **wav2vec2** -- [Wav2Vec2Config](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2Config) (Wav2Vec2 model)
- **xlm** -- [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) (XLM model)
- **xlm-prophetnet** -- [XLMProphetNetConfig](model_doc/xlmprophetnet.html#transformers.XLMProphetNetConfig) (XLMProphetNet model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) (XLNet model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model configuration hosted inside a model repo on
    huggingface.co. Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or
    namespaced under a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing a configuration file saved using the
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.save_pretrained) method, or the
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) method, e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a saved configuration JSON _file_, e.g.,
    `./my_model_directory/configuration.json`.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download the model weights and configuration files and override the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **return_unused_kwargs** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  If `False`, then this function returns just the final configuration object.

  If `True`, then this functions returns a `Tuple(config, unused_kwargs)` where _unused_kwargs_
  is a dictionary consisting of the key/value pairs whose keys are not configuration attributes: i.e.,
  the part of `kwargs` which has not been used to update `config` and is otherwise ignored.
- **kwargs(additional** keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  The values in kwargs of any keys which are configuration attributes will be used to override the loaded
  values. Behavior concerning key/value pairs whose keys are *not* configuration attributes is controlled
  by the `return_unused_kwargs` keyword parameter.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig

>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-uncased')

>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co (user-uploaded) and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased')

>>> # If configuration file is in a directory (e.g., was saved using _save_pretrained('./test/saved_model/')_).
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./test/bert_saved_model/')

>>> # Load a specific configuration file.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./test/bert_saved_model/my_configuration.json')

>>> # Change some config attributes when loading a pretrained config.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-uncased', output_attentions=True, foo=False)
>>> config.output_attentions
True
>>> config, unused_kwargs = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-uncased', output_attentions=True, foo=False, return_unused_kwargs=True)
>>> config.output_attentions
True
>>> config.unused_kwargs
&lcub'foo': False}
```


## AutoTokenizer

<a id='transformers.AutoTokenizer'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoTokenizer**()


This is a generic tokenizer class that will be instantiated as one of the tokenizer classes of the library when
created with the [AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained()](model_doc/auto.html#transformers.AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained) class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(pretrained_model_name_or_path, *inputs, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the tokenizer classes of the library from a pretrained model vocabulary.

The tokenizer class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object
(either passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's
missing, by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [AlbertTokenizer](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertTokenizer) or [AlbertTokenizerFast](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertTokenizerFast) (ALBERT model)
- **bart** -- [BartTokenizer](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartTokenizer) or [BartTokenizerFast](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartTokenizerFast) (BART model)
- **barthez** -- [BarthezTokenizer](model_doc/barthez.html#transformers.BarthezTokenizer) or [BarthezTokenizerFast](model_doc/barthez.html#transformers.BarthezTokenizerFast) (BARThez model)
- **bert** -- [BertTokenizer](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertTokenizer) or [BertTokenizerFast](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertTokenizerFast) (BERT model)
- **bert-generation** -- [BertGenerationTokenizer](model_doc/bertgeneration.html#transformers.BertGenerationTokenizer) (Bert Generation model)
- **bert-japanese** -- [BertJapaneseTokenizer](model_doc/bert_japanese.html#transformers.BertJapaneseTokenizer) (BertJapanese model)
- **bertweet** -- [BertweetTokenizer](model_doc/bertweet.html#transformers.BertweetTokenizer) (Bertweet model)
- **big_bird** -- [BigBirdTokenizer](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdTokenizer) or [BigBirdTokenizerFast](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdTokenizerFast) (BigBird model)
- **bigbird_pegasus** -- [PegasusTokenizer](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusTokenizer) or [PegasusTokenizerFast](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusTokenizerFast) (BigBirdPegasus model)
- **blenderbot** -- [BlenderbotTokenizer](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.BlenderbotTokenizer) (Blenderbot model)
- **blenderbot-small** -- [BlenderbotSmallTokenizer](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.BlenderbotSmallTokenizer) (BlenderbotSmall model)
- **byt5** -- [ByT5Tokenizer](model_doc/byt5.html#transformers.ByT5Tokenizer) (ByT5 model)
- **camembert** -- [CamembertTokenizer](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertTokenizer) or [CamembertTokenizerFast](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertTokenizerFast) (CamemBERT model)
- **canine** -- [CanineTokenizer](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineTokenizer) (Canine model)
- **clip** -- [CLIPTokenizer](model_doc/clip.html#transformers.CLIPTokenizer) or [CLIPTokenizerFast](model_doc/clip.html#transformers.CLIPTokenizerFast) (CLIP model)
- **convbert** -- [ConvBertTokenizer](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertTokenizer) or [ConvBertTokenizerFast](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertTokenizerFast) (ConvBERT model)
- **cpm** -- [CpmTokenizer](model_doc/cpm.html#transformers.CpmTokenizer) or `CpmTokenizerFast` (CPM model)
- **ctrl** -- [CTRLTokenizer](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLTokenizer) (CTRL model)
- **deberta** -- [DebertaTokenizer](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaTokenizer) or [DebertaTokenizerFast](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaTokenizerFast) (DeBERTa model)
- **deberta-v2** -- [DebertaV2Tokenizer](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Tokenizer) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
- **distilbert** -- [DistilBertTokenizer](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertTokenizer) or [DistilBertTokenizerFast](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertTokenizerFast) (DistilBERT model)
- **dpr** -- [DPRQuestionEncoderTokenizer](model_doc/dpr.html#transformers.DPRQuestionEncoderTokenizer) or [DPRQuestionEncoderTokenizerFast](model_doc/dpr.html#transformers.DPRQuestionEncoderTokenizerFast) (DPR model)
- **electra** -- [ElectraTokenizer](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraTokenizer) or [ElectraTokenizerFast](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraTokenizerFast) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [FlaubertTokenizer](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertTokenizer) (FlauBERT model)
- **fnet** -- [FNetTokenizer](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetTokenizer) or [FNetTokenizerFast](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetTokenizerFast) (FNet model)
- **fsmt** -- [FSMTTokenizer](model_doc/fsmt.html#transformers.FSMTTokenizer) (FairSeq Machine-Translation model)
- **funnel** -- [FunnelTokenizer](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelTokenizer) or [FunnelTokenizerFast](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelTokenizerFast) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **gpt2** -- [GPT2Tokenizer](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Tokenizer) or [GPT2TokenizerFast](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2TokenizerFast) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
- **gpt_neo** -- [GPT2Tokenizer](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Tokenizer) or [GPT2TokenizerFast](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2TokenizerFast) (GPT Neo model)
- **hubert** -- [Wav2Vec2CTCTokenizer](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2CTCTokenizer) (Hubert model)
- **ibert** -- [RobertaTokenizer](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaTokenizer) or [RobertaTokenizerFast](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaTokenizerFast) (I-BERT model)
- **layoutlm** -- [LayoutLMTokenizer](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMTokenizer) or [LayoutLMTokenizerFast](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMTokenizerFast) (LayoutLM model)
- **layoutlmv2** -- [LayoutLMv2Tokenizer](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2Tokenizer) or [LayoutLMv2TokenizerFast](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2TokenizerFast) (LayoutLMv2 model)
- **led** -- [LEDTokenizer](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDTokenizer) or [LEDTokenizerFast](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDTokenizerFast) (LED model)
- **longformer** -- [LongformerTokenizer](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerTokenizer) or [LongformerTokenizerFast](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerTokenizerFast) (Longformer model)
- **luke** -- [LukeTokenizer](model_doc/luke.html#transformers.LukeTokenizer) (LUKE model)
- **lxmert** -- [LxmertTokenizer](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertTokenizer) or [LxmertTokenizerFast](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertTokenizerFast) (LXMERT model)
- **m2m_100** -- [M2M100Tokenizer](model_doc/m2m_100.html#transformers.M2M100Tokenizer) (M2M100 model)
- **marian** -- [MarianTokenizer](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianTokenizer) (Marian model)
- **mbart** -- [MBartTokenizer](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartTokenizer) or [MBartTokenizerFast](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartTokenizerFast) (mBART model)
- **mbart50** -- [MBart50Tokenizer](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBart50Tokenizer) or [MBart50TokenizerFast](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBart50TokenizerFast) (mBART-50 model)
- **mobilebert** -- [MobileBertTokenizer](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertTokenizer) or [MobileBertTokenizerFast](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertTokenizerFast) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [MPNetTokenizer](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetTokenizer) or [MPNetTokenizerFast](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetTokenizerFast) (MPNet model)
- **mt5** -- [MT5Tokenizer](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Tokenizer) or [MT5TokenizerFast](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5TokenizerFast) (mT5 model)
- **openai-gpt** -- [OpenAIGPTTokenizer](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTTokenizer) or [OpenAIGPTTokenizerFast](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTTokenizerFast) (OpenAI GPT model)
- **pegasus** -- [PegasusTokenizer](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusTokenizer) or [PegasusTokenizerFast](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusTokenizerFast) (Pegasus model)
- **phobert** -- [PhobertTokenizer](model_doc/phobert.html#transformers.PhobertTokenizer) (PhoBERT model)
- **prophetnet** -- [ProphetNetTokenizer](model_doc/prophetnet.html#transformers.ProphetNetTokenizer) (ProphetNet model)
- **rag** -- [RagTokenizer](model_doc/rag.html#transformers.RagTokenizer) (RAG model)
- **reformer** -- [ReformerTokenizer](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerTokenizer) or [ReformerTokenizerFast](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerTokenizerFast) (Reformer model)
- **rembert** -- [RemBertTokenizer](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertTokenizer) or [RemBertTokenizerFast](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertTokenizerFast) (RemBERT model)
- **retribert** -- [RetriBertTokenizer](model_doc/retribert.html#transformers.RetriBertTokenizer) or [RetriBertTokenizerFast](model_doc/retribert.html#transformers.RetriBertTokenizerFast) (RetriBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [RobertaTokenizer](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaTokenizer) or [RobertaTokenizerFast](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaTokenizerFast) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [RoFormerTokenizer](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerTokenizer) or [RoFormerTokenizerFast](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerTokenizerFast) (RoFormer model)
- **speech_to_text** -- [Speech2TextTokenizer](model_doc/speech_to_text.html#transformers.Speech2TextTokenizer) (Speech2Text model)
- **speech_to_text_2** -- [Speech2Text2Tokenizer](model_doc/speech_to_text_2.html#transformers.Speech2Text2Tokenizer) (Speech2Text2 model)
- **splinter** -- [SplinterTokenizer](model_doc/splinter.html#transformers.SplinterTokenizer) or [SplinterTokenizerFast](model_doc/splinter.html#transformers.SplinterTokenizerFast) (Splinter model)
- **squeezebert** -- [SqueezeBertTokenizer](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertTokenizer) or [SqueezeBertTokenizerFast](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertTokenizerFast) (SqueezeBERT model)
- **t5** -- [T5Tokenizer](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Tokenizer) or [T5TokenizerFast](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5TokenizerFast) (T5 model)
- **tapas** -- [TapasTokenizer](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasTokenizer) (TAPAS model)
- **transfo-xl** -- [TransfoXLTokenizer](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLTokenizer) (Transformer-XL model)
- **wav2vec2** -- [Wav2Vec2CTCTokenizer](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2CTCTokenizer) (Wav2Vec2 model)
- **xlm** -- [XLMTokenizer](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMTokenizer) (XLM model)
- **xlm-prophetnet** -- [XLMProphetNetTokenizer](model_doc/xlmprophetnet.html#transformers.XLMProphetNetTokenizer) (XLMProphetNet model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [XLMRobertaTokenizer](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaTokenizer) or [XLMRobertaTokenizerFast](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaTokenizerFast) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [XLNetTokenizer](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetTokenizer) or [XLNetTokenizerFast](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetTokenizerFast) (XLNet model)

Params:
pretrained_model_name_or_path (`str` or `os.PathLike`):
Can be either:

- A string, the _model id_ of a predefined tokenizer hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
  Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
  a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
- A path to a _directory_ containing vocabulary files required by the tokenizer, for instance saved
  using the [save_pretrained()](internal/tokenization_utils.html#transformers.PreTrainedTokenizerBase.save_pretrained) method, e.g.,
  `./my_model_directory/`.
- A path or url to a single saved vocabulary file if and only if the tokenizer only requires a
  single vocabulary file (like Bert or XLNet), e.g.: `./my_model_directory/vocab.txt`. (Not
  applicable to all derived classes)
inputs (additional positional arguments, _optional_):
Will be passed along to the Tokenizer `__init__()` method.
config ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_)
The configuration object used to dertermine the tokenizer class to instantiate.
cache_dir (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_):
Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
standard cache should not be used.
force_download (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`):
Whether or not to force the (re-)download the model weights and configuration files and override the
cached versions if they exist.
resume_download (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`):
Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
file exists.
proxies (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_):
A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
revision(`str`, _optional_, defaults to `"main"`):
The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
identifier allowed by git.
subfolder (`str`, _optional_):
In case the relevant files are located inside a subfolder of the model repo on huggingface.co (e.g. for
facebook/rag-token-base), specify it here.
use_fast (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `True`):
Whether or not to try to load the fast version of the tokenizer.
tokenizer_type (`str`, _optional_):
Tokenizer type to be loaded.
kwargs (additional keyword arguments, _optional_):
Will be passed to the Tokenizer `__init__()` method. Can be used to set special tokens like
`bos_token`, `eos_token`, `unk_token`, `sep_token`, `pad_token`, `cls_token`,
`mask_token`, `additional_special_tokens`. See parameters in the `__init__()` for more details.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoTokenizer

>>> # Download vocabulary from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained('bert-base-uncased')

>>> # Download vocabulary from huggingface.co (user-uploaded) and cache.
>>> tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained('dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased')

>>> # If vocabulary files are in a directory (e.g. tokenizer was saved using _save_pretrained('./test/saved_model/')_)
>>> tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained('./test/bert_saved_model/')
```


## AutoFeatureExtractor

<a id='transformers.AutoFeatureExtractor'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoFeatureExtractor**()


This is a generic feature extractor class that will be instantiated as one of the feature extractor classes of the
library when created with the [AutoFeatureExtractor.from_pretrained()](model_doc/auto.html#transformers.AutoFeatureExtractor.from_pretrained) class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.AutoFeatureExtractor.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(pretrained_model_name_or_path, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the feature extractor classes of the library from a pretrained model vocabulary.

The tokenizer class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object
(either passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's
missing, by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **beit** -- [BeitFeatureExtractor](model_doc/beit.html#transformers.BeitFeatureExtractor) (BeiT model)
- **clip** -- [CLIPFeatureExtractor](model_doc/clip.html#transformers.CLIPFeatureExtractor) (CLIP model)
- **deit** -- [DeiTFeatureExtractor](model_doc/deit.html#transformers.DeiTFeatureExtractor) (DeiT model)
- **detr** -- [DetrFeatureExtractor](model_doc/detr.html#transformers.DetrFeatureExtractor) (DETR model)
- **hubert** -- [Wav2Vec2FeatureExtractor](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2FeatureExtractor) (Hubert model)
- **layoutlmv2** -- [LayoutLMv2FeatureExtractor](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2FeatureExtractor) (LayoutLMv2 model)
- **speech_to_text** -- [Speech2TextFeatureExtractor](model_doc/speech_to_text.html#transformers.Speech2TextFeatureExtractor) (Speech2Text model)
- **vit** -- [ViTFeatureExtractor](model_doc/vit.html#transformers.ViTFeatureExtractor) (ViT model)
- **wav2vec2** -- [Wav2Vec2FeatureExtractor](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2FeatureExtractor) (Wav2Vec2 model)

Params:
pretrained_model_name_or_path (`str` or `os.PathLike`):
This can be either:

- a string, the _model id_ of a pretrained feature_extractor hosted inside a model repo on
  huggingface.co. Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or
  namespaced under a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
- a path to a _directory_ containing a feature extractor file saved using the
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/feature_extractor.html#transformers.feature_extraction_utils.FeatureExtractionMixin.save_pretrained) method, e.g.,
  `./my_model_directory/`.
- a path or url to a saved feature extractor JSON _file_, e.g.,
  `./my_model_directory/preprocessor_config.json`.
cache_dir (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_):
Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model feature extractor should be cached if the
standard cache should not be used.
force_download (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`):
Whether or not to force to (re-)download the feature extractor files and override the cached versions
if they exist.
resume_download (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`):
Whether or not to delete incompletely received file. Attempts to resume the download if such a file
exists.
proxies (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_):
A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}.` The proxies are used on each request.
use_auth_token (`str` or _bool_, _optional_):
The token to use as HTTP bearer authorization for remote files. If `True`, will use the token
generated when running `transformers-cli login` (stored in `~/.huggingface`).
revision(`str`, _optional_, defaults to `"main"`):
The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
identifier allowed by git.
return_unused_kwargs (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`):
If `False`, then this function returns just the final feature extractor object. If `True`,
then this functions returns a `Tuple(feature_extractor, unused_kwargs)` where _unused_kwargs_ is a
dictionary consisting of the key/value pairs whose keys are not feature extractor attributes: i.e., the
part of `kwargs` which has not been used to update `feature_extractor` and is otherwise ignored.
kwargs (`Dict[str, Any]`, _optional_):
The values in kwargs of any keys which are feature extractor attributes will be used to override the
loaded values. Behavior concerning key/value pairs whose keys are *not* feature extractor attributes is
controlled by the `return_unused_kwargs` keyword parameter.

<Tip>

Passing `use_auth_token=True` is required when you want to use a private model.

</Tip>

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoFeatureExtractor

>>> # Download vocabulary from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> feature_extractor = AutoFeatureExtractor.from_pretrained('facebook/wav2vec2-base-960h')

>>> # If vocabulary files are in a directory (e.g. feature extractor was saved using _save_pretrained('./test/saved_model/')_)
>>> feature_extractor = AutoFeatureExtractor.from_pretrained('./test/saved_model/')
```


## AutoModel

<a id='transformers.AutoModel'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModel**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the base model classes of the library when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the base model classes of the library from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [AlbertModel](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertModel) (ALBERT model)
  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [BartModel](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartModel) (BART model)
  - [BeitConfig](model_doc/beit.html#transformers.BeitConfig) configuration class: [BeitModel](model_doc/beit.html#transformers.BeitModel) (BeiT model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [BertModel](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertModel) (BERT model)
  - [BertGenerationConfig](model_doc/bertgeneration.html#transformers.BertGenerationConfig) configuration class: [BertGenerationEncoder](model_doc/bertgeneration.html#transformers.BertGenerationEncoder) (Bert Generation model)
  - [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) configuration class: [BigBirdModel](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdModel) (BigBird model)
  - [BigBirdPegasusConfig](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusConfig) configuration class: [BigBirdPegasusModel](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusModel) (BigBirdPegasus model)
  - [BlenderbotConfig](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.BlenderbotConfig) configuration class: [BlenderbotModel](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.BlenderbotModel) (Blenderbot model)
  - [BlenderbotSmallConfig](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.BlenderbotSmallConfig) configuration class: [BlenderbotSmallModel](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.BlenderbotSmallModel) (BlenderbotSmall model)
  - [CLIPConfig](model_doc/clip.html#transformers.CLIPConfig) configuration class: [CLIPModel](model_doc/clip.html#transformers.CLIPModel) (CLIP model)
  - [CTRLConfig](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLConfig) configuration class: [CTRLModel](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLModel) (CTRL model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [CamembertModel](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertModel) (CamemBERT model)
  - [CanineConfig](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineConfig) configuration class: [CanineModel](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineModel) (Canine model)
  - [ConvBertConfig](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertConfig) configuration class: [ConvBertModel](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertModel) (ConvBERT model)
  - [DPRConfig](model_doc/dpr.html#transformers.DPRConfig) configuration class: [DPRQuestionEncoder](model_doc/dpr.html#transformers.DPRQuestionEncoder) (DPR model)
  - [DebertaConfig](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaConfig) configuration class: [DebertaModel](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaModel) (DeBERTa model)
  - [DebertaV2Config](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Config) configuration class: [DebertaV2Model](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Model) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
  - [DeiTConfig](model_doc/deit.html#transformers.DeiTConfig) configuration class: [DeiTModel](model_doc/deit.html#transformers.DeiTModel) (DeiT model)
  - [DetrConfig](model_doc/detr.html#transformers.DetrConfig) configuration class: [DetrModel](model_doc/detr.html#transformers.DetrModel) (DETR model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [DistilBertModel](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertModel) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [ElectraModel](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraModel) (ELECTRA model)
  - [FNetConfig](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetConfig) configuration class: [FNetModel](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetModel) (FNet model)
  - [FSMTConfig](model_doc/fsmt.html#transformers.FSMTConfig) configuration class: [FSMTModel](model_doc/fsmt.html#transformers.FSMTModel) (FairSeq Machine-Translation model)
  - [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) configuration class: [FlaubertModel](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertModel) (FlauBERT model)
  - [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) configuration class: [FunnelModel](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelModel) or [FunnelBaseModel](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelBaseModel) (Funnel Transformer model)
  - [GPT2Config](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Config) configuration class: [GPT2Model](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Model) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
  - [GPTJConfig](model_doc/gptj.html#transformers.GPTJConfig) configuration class: [GPTJModel](model_doc/gptj.html#transformers.GPTJModel) (GPT-J model)
  - [GPTNeoConfig](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.GPTNeoConfig) configuration class: [GPTNeoModel](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.GPTNeoModel) (GPT Neo model)
  - [HubertConfig](model_doc/hubert.html#transformers.HubertConfig) configuration class: [HubertModel](model_doc/hubert.html#transformers.HubertModel) (Hubert model)
  - [IBertConfig](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertConfig) configuration class: [IBertModel](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertModel) (I-BERT model)
  - [LEDConfig](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDConfig) configuration class: [LEDModel](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDModel) (LED model)
  - [LayoutLMConfig](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMConfig) configuration class: [LayoutLMModel](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMModel) (LayoutLM model)
  - [LayoutLMv2Config](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2Config) configuration class: [LayoutLMv2Model](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2Model) (LayoutLMv2 model)
  - [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) configuration class: [LongformerModel](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerModel) (Longformer model)
  - [LukeConfig](model_doc/luke.html#transformers.LukeConfig) configuration class: [LukeModel](model_doc/luke.html#transformers.LukeModel) (LUKE model)
  - [LxmertConfig](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertConfig) configuration class: [LxmertModel](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertModel) (LXMERT model)
  - [M2M100Config](model_doc/m2m_100.html#transformers.M2M100Config) configuration class: [M2M100Model](model_doc/m2m_100.html#transformers.M2M100Model) (M2M100 model)
  - [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) configuration class: [MBartModel](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartModel) (mBART model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [MPNetModel](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetModel) (MPNet model)
  - [MT5Config](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.MT5Config) configuration class: [MT5Model](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.MT5Model) (mT5 model)
  - [MarianConfig](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianConfig) configuration class: [MarianModel](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianModel) (Marian model)
  - [MegatronBertConfig](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertConfig) configuration class: [MegatronBertModel](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertModel) (MegatronBert model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [MobileBertModel](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertModel) (MobileBERT model)
  - [OpenAIGPTConfig](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTConfig) configuration class: [OpenAIGPTModel](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTModel) (OpenAI GPT model)
  - [PegasusConfig](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusConfig) configuration class: [PegasusModel](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusModel) (Pegasus model)
  - [ProphetNetConfig](model_doc/prophetnet.html#transformers.ProphetNetConfig) configuration class: [ProphetNetModel](model_doc/prophetnet.html#transformers.ProphetNetModel) (ProphetNet model)
  - [ReformerConfig](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerConfig) configuration class: [ReformerModel](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerModel) (Reformer model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [RemBertModel](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertModel) (RemBERT model)
  - [RetriBertConfig](model_doc/retribert.html#transformers.RetriBertConfig) configuration class: [RetriBertModel](model_doc/retribert.html#transformers.RetriBertModel) (RetriBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [RoFormerModel](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerModel) (RoFormer model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [RobertaModel](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaModel) (RoBERTa model)
  - [Speech2TextConfig](model_doc/speech_to_text.html#transformers.Speech2TextConfig) configuration class: [Speech2TextModel](model_doc/speech_to_text.html#transformers.Speech2TextModel) (Speech2Text model)
  - [SplinterConfig](model_doc/splinter.html#transformers.SplinterConfig) configuration class: [SplinterModel](model_doc/splinter.html#transformers.SplinterModel) (Splinter model)
  - [SqueezeBertConfig](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertConfig) configuration class: [SqueezeBertModel](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertModel) (SqueezeBERT model)
  - [T5Config](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Config) configuration class: [T5Model](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Model) (T5 model)
  - [TapasConfig](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasConfig) configuration class: [TapasModel](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasModel) (TAPAS model)
  - [TransfoXLConfig](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLConfig) configuration class: [TransfoXLModel](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLModel) (Transformer-XL model)
  - [ViTConfig](model_doc/vit.html#transformers.ViTConfig) configuration class: [ViTModel](model_doc/vit.html#transformers.ViTModel) (ViT model)
  - [VisualBertConfig](model_doc/visual_bert.html#transformers.VisualBertConfig) configuration class: [VisualBertModel](model_doc/visual_bert.html#transformers.VisualBertModel) (VisualBert model)
  - [Wav2Vec2Config](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2Config) configuration class: [Wav2Vec2Model](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2Model) (Wav2Vec2 model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [XLMModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMModel) (XLM model)
  - [XLMProphetNetConfig](model_doc/xlmprophetnet.html#transformers.XLMProphetNetConfig) configuration class: [XLMProphetNetModel](model_doc/xlmprophetnet.html#transformers.XLMProphetNetModel) (XLMProphetNet model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [XLMRobertaModel](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaModel) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [XLNetModel](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetModel) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModel
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = AutoModel.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the base model classes of the library from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [AlbertModel](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertModel) (ALBERT model)
- **bart** -- [BartModel](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartModel) (BART model)
- **beit** -- [BeitModel](model_doc/beit.html#transformers.BeitModel) (BeiT model)
- **bert** -- [BertModel](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertModel) (BERT model)
- **bert-generation** -- [BertGenerationEncoder](model_doc/bertgeneration.html#transformers.BertGenerationEncoder) (Bert Generation model)
- **big_bird** -- [BigBirdModel](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdModel) (BigBird model)
- **bigbird_pegasus** -- [BigBirdPegasusModel](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusModel) (BigBirdPegasus model)
- **blenderbot** -- [BlenderbotModel](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.BlenderbotModel) (Blenderbot model)
- **blenderbot-small** -- [BlenderbotSmallModel](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.BlenderbotSmallModel) (BlenderbotSmall model)
- **camembert** -- [CamembertModel](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertModel) (CamemBERT model)
- **canine** -- [CanineModel](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineModel) (Canine model)
- **clip** -- [CLIPModel](model_doc/clip.html#transformers.CLIPModel) (CLIP model)
- **convbert** -- [ConvBertModel](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertModel) (ConvBERT model)
- **ctrl** -- [CTRLModel](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLModel) (CTRL model)
- **deberta** -- [DebertaModel](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaModel) (DeBERTa model)
- **deberta-v2** -- [DebertaV2Model](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Model) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
- **deit** -- [DeiTModel](model_doc/deit.html#transformers.DeiTModel) (DeiT model)
- **detr** -- [DetrModel](model_doc/detr.html#transformers.DetrModel) (DETR model)
- **distilbert** -- [DistilBertModel](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertModel) (DistilBERT model)
- **dpr** -- [DPRQuestionEncoder](model_doc/dpr.html#transformers.DPRQuestionEncoder) (DPR model)
- **electra** -- [ElectraModel](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraModel) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [FlaubertModel](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertModel) (FlauBERT model)
- **fnet** -- [FNetModel](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetModel) (FNet model)
- **fsmt** -- [FSMTModel](model_doc/fsmt.html#transformers.FSMTModel) (FairSeq Machine-Translation model)
- **funnel** -- [FunnelModel](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelModel) or [FunnelBaseModel](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelBaseModel) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **gpt2** -- [GPT2Model](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Model) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
- **gpt_neo** -- [GPTNeoModel](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.GPTNeoModel) (GPT Neo model)
- **gptj** -- [GPTJModel](model_doc/gptj.html#transformers.GPTJModel) (GPT-J model)
- **hubert** -- [HubertModel](model_doc/hubert.html#transformers.HubertModel) (Hubert model)
- **ibert** -- [IBertModel](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertModel) (I-BERT model)
- **layoutlm** -- [LayoutLMModel](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMModel) (LayoutLM model)
- **layoutlmv2** -- [LayoutLMv2Model](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2Model) (LayoutLMv2 model)
- **led** -- [LEDModel](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDModel) (LED model)
- **longformer** -- [LongformerModel](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerModel) (Longformer model)
- **luke** -- [LukeModel](model_doc/luke.html#transformers.LukeModel) (LUKE model)
- **lxmert** -- [LxmertModel](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertModel) (LXMERT model)
- **m2m_100** -- [M2M100Model](model_doc/m2m_100.html#transformers.M2M100Model) (M2M100 model)
- **marian** -- [MarianModel](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianModel) (Marian model)
- **mbart** -- [MBartModel](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartModel) (mBART model)
- **megatron-bert** -- [MegatronBertModel](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertModel) (MegatronBert model)
- **mobilebert** -- [MobileBertModel](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertModel) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [MPNetModel](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetModel) (MPNet model)
- **mt5** -- [MT5Model](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.MT5Model) (mT5 model)
- **openai-gpt** -- [OpenAIGPTModel](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTModel) (OpenAI GPT model)
- **pegasus** -- [PegasusModel](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusModel) (Pegasus model)
- **prophetnet** -- [ProphetNetModel](model_doc/prophetnet.html#transformers.ProphetNetModel) (ProphetNet model)
- **reformer** -- [ReformerModel](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerModel) (Reformer model)
- **rembert** -- [RemBertModel](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertModel) (RemBERT model)
- **retribert** -- [RetriBertModel](model_doc/retribert.html#transformers.RetriBertModel) (RetriBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [RobertaModel](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaModel) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [RoFormerModel](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerModel) (RoFormer model)
- **speech_to_text** -- [Speech2TextModel](model_doc/speech_to_text.html#transformers.Speech2TextModel) (Speech2Text model)
- **splinter** -- [SplinterModel](model_doc/splinter.html#transformers.SplinterModel) (Splinter model)
- **squeezebert** -- [SqueezeBertModel](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertModel) (SqueezeBERT model)
- **t5** -- [T5Model](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Model) (T5 model)
- **tapas** -- [TapasModel](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasModel) (TAPAS model)
- **transfo-xl** -- [TransfoXLModel](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLModel) (Transformer-XL model)
- **visual_bert** -- [VisualBertModel](model_doc/visual_bert.html#transformers.VisualBertModel) (VisualBert model)
- **vit** -- [ViTModel](model_doc/vit.html#transformers.ViTModel) (ViT model)
- **wav2vec2** -- [Wav2Vec2Model](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2Model) (Wav2Vec2 model)
- **xlm** -- [XLMModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMModel) (XLM model)
- **xlm-prophetnet** -- [XLMProphetNetModel](model_doc/xlmprophetnet.html#transformers.XLMProphetNetModel) (XLMProphetNet model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [XLMRobertaModel](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaModel) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [XLNetModel](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetModel) (XLNet model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModel

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModel.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModel.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModel.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```


## AutoModelForPreTraining

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForPreTraining'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForPreTraining**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a pretraining head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a pretraining head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [AlbertForPreTraining](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertForPreTraining) (ALBERT model)
  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [BartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [BertForPreTraining](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForPreTraining) (BERT model)
  - [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) configuration class: [BigBirdForPreTraining](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForPreTraining) (BigBird model)
  - [CTRLConfig](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLConfig) configuration class: [CTRLLMHeadModel](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLLMHeadModel) (CTRL model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [CamembertForMaskedLM](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForMaskedLM) (CamemBERT model)
  - [DebertaConfig](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaConfig) configuration class: [DebertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaForMaskedLM) (DeBERTa model)
  - [DebertaV2Config](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Config) configuration class: [DebertaV2ForMaskedLM](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2ForMaskedLM) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [DistilBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertForMaskedLM) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [ElectraForPreTraining](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraForPreTraining) (ELECTRA model)
  - [FNetConfig](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetConfig) configuration class: [FNetForPreTraining](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForPreTraining) (FNet model)
  - [FSMTConfig](model_doc/fsmt.html#transformers.FSMTConfig) configuration class: [FSMTForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/fsmt.html#transformers.FSMTForConditionalGeneration) (FairSeq Machine-Translation model)
  - [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) configuration class: [FlaubertWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertWithLMHeadModel) (FlauBERT model)
  - [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) configuration class: [FunnelForPreTraining](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelForPreTraining) (Funnel Transformer model)
  - [GPT2Config](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Config) configuration class: [GPT2LMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2LMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
  - [IBertConfig](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertConfig) configuration class: [IBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertForMaskedLM) (I-BERT model)
  - [LayoutLMConfig](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMConfig) configuration class: [LayoutLMForMaskedLM](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMForMaskedLM) (LayoutLM model)
  - [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) configuration class: [LongformerForMaskedLM](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerForMaskedLM) (Longformer model)
  - [LxmertConfig](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertConfig) configuration class: [LxmertForPreTraining](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertForPreTraining) (LXMERT model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [MPNetForMaskedLM](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetForMaskedLM) (MPNet model)
  - [MegatronBertConfig](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertConfig) configuration class: [MegatronBertForPreTraining](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForPreTraining) (MegatronBert model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [MobileBertForPreTraining](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForPreTraining) (MobileBERT model)
  - [OpenAIGPTConfig](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTConfig) configuration class: [OpenAIGPTLMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTLMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT model)
  - [RetriBertConfig](model_doc/retribert.html#transformers.RetriBertConfig) configuration class: [RetriBertModel](model_doc/retribert.html#transformers.RetriBertModel) (RetriBERT model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [RobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForMaskedLM) (RoBERTa model)
  - [SqueezeBertConfig](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertConfig) configuration class: [SqueezeBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertForMaskedLM) (SqueezeBERT model)
  - [T5Config](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Config) configuration class: [T5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5ForConditionalGeneration) (T5 model)
  - [TapasConfig](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasConfig) configuration class: [TapasForMaskedLM](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasForMaskedLM) (TAPAS model)
  - [TransfoXLConfig](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLConfig) configuration class: [TransfoXLLMHeadModel](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLLMHeadModel) (Transformer-XL model)
  - [VisualBertConfig](model_doc/visual_bert.html#transformers.VisualBertConfig) configuration class: [VisualBertForPreTraining](model_doc/visual_bert.html#transformers.VisualBertForPreTraining) (VisualBert model)
  - [Wav2Vec2Config](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2Config) configuration class: [Wav2Vec2ForPreTraining](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2ForPreTraining) (Wav2Vec2 model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [XLMWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMWithLMHeadModel) (XLM model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [XLMRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForMaskedLM) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [XLNetLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetLMHeadModel) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForPreTraining
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = AutoModelForPreTraining.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a pretraining head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [AlbertForPreTraining](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertForPreTraining) (ALBERT model)
- **bart** -- [BartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
- **bert** -- [BertForPreTraining](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForPreTraining) (BERT model)
- **big_bird** -- [BigBirdForPreTraining](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForPreTraining) (BigBird model)
- **camembert** -- [CamembertForMaskedLM](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForMaskedLM) (CamemBERT model)
- **ctrl** -- [CTRLLMHeadModel](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLLMHeadModel) (CTRL model)
- **deberta** -- [DebertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaForMaskedLM) (DeBERTa model)
- **deberta-v2** -- [DebertaV2ForMaskedLM](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2ForMaskedLM) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
- **distilbert** -- [DistilBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertForMaskedLM) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [ElectraForPreTraining](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraForPreTraining) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [FlaubertWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertWithLMHeadModel) (FlauBERT model)
- **fnet** -- [FNetForPreTraining](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForPreTraining) (FNet model)
- **fsmt** -- [FSMTForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/fsmt.html#transformers.FSMTForConditionalGeneration) (FairSeq Machine-Translation model)
- **funnel** -- [FunnelForPreTraining](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelForPreTraining) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **gpt2** -- [GPT2LMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2LMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
- **ibert** -- [IBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertForMaskedLM) (I-BERT model)
- **layoutlm** -- [LayoutLMForMaskedLM](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMForMaskedLM) (LayoutLM model)
- **longformer** -- [LongformerForMaskedLM](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerForMaskedLM) (Longformer model)
- **lxmert** -- [LxmertForPreTraining](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertForPreTraining) (LXMERT model)
- **megatron-bert** -- [MegatronBertForPreTraining](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForPreTraining) (MegatronBert model)
- **mobilebert** -- [MobileBertForPreTraining](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForPreTraining) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [MPNetForMaskedLM](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetForMaskedLM) (MPNet model)
- **openai-gpt** -- [OpenAIGPTLMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTLMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT model)
- **retribert** -- [RetriBertModel](model_doc/retribert.html#transformers.RetriBertModel) (RetriBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [RobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForMaskedLM) (RoBERTa model)
- **squeezebert** -- [SqueezeBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertForMaskedLM) (SqueezeBERT model)
- **t5** -- [T5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5ForConditionalGeneration) (T5 model)
- **tapas** -- [TapasForMaskedLM](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasForMaskedLM) (TAPAS model)
- **transfo-xl** -- [TransfoXLLMHeadModel](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLLMHeadModel) (Transformer-XL model)
- **visual_bert** -- [VisualBertForPreTraining](model_doc/visual_bert.html#transformers.VisualBertForPreTraining) (VisualBert model)
- **wav2vec2** -- [Wav2Vec2ForPreTraining](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2ForPreTraining) (Wav2Vec2 model)
- **xlm** -- [XLMWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMWithLMHeadModel) (XLM model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [XLMRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForMaskedLM) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [XLNetLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetLMHeadModel) (XLNet model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForPreTraining

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForPreTraining.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForPreTraining.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModelForPreTraining.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```


## AutoModelForCausalLM

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForCausalLM'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForCausalLM**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a causal language modeling head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a causal language modeling head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [BartForCausalLM](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartForCausalLM) (BART model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [BertLMHeadModel](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertLMHeadModel) (BERT model)
  - [BertGenerationConfig](model_doc/bertgeneration.html#transformers.BertGenerationConfig) configuration class: [BertGenerationDecoder](model_doc/bertgeneration.html#transformers.BertGenerationDecoder) (Bert Generation model)
  - [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) configuration class: [BigBirdForCausalLM](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForCausalLM) (BigBird model)
  - [BigBirdPegasusConfig](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusConfig) configuration class: [BigBirdPegasusForCausalLM](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusForCausalLM) (BigBirdPegasus model)
  - [BlenderbotConfig](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.BlenderbotConfig) configuration class: [BlenderbotForCausalLM](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.BlenderbotForCausalLM) (Blenderbot model)
  - [BlenderbotSmallConfig](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.BlenderbotSmallConfig) configuration class: [BlenderbotSmallForCausalLM](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.BlenderbotSmallForCausalLM) (BlenderbotSmall model)
  - [CTRLConfig](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLConfig) configuration class: [CTRLLMHeadModel](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLLMHeadModel) (CTRL model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [CamembertForCausalLM](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForCausalLM) (CamemBERT model)
  - [GPT2Config](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Config) configuration class: [GPT2LMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2LMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
  - [GPTJConfig](model_doc/gptj.html#transformers.GPTJConfig) configuration class: [GPTJForCausalLM](model_doc/gptj.html#transformers.GPTJForCausalLM) (GPT-J model)
