  - [GPTNeoConfig](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.GPTNeoConfig) configuration class: [GPTNeoForCausalLM](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.GPTNeoForCausalLM) (GPT Neo model)
  - [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) configuration class: [MBartForCausalLM](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartForCausalLM) (mBART model)
  - [MarianConfig](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianConfig) configuration class: [MarianForCausalLM](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianForCausalLM) (Marian model)
  - [MegatronBertConfig](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertConfig) configuration class: [MegatronBertForCausalLM](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForCausalLM) (MegatronBert model)
  - [OpenAIGPTConfig](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTConfig) configuration class: [OpenAIGPTLMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTLMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT model)
  - [PegasusConfig](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusConfig) configuration class: [PegasusForCausalLM](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusForCausalLM) (Pegasus model)
  - [ProphetNetConfig](model_doc/prophetnet.html#transformers.ProphetNetConfig) configuration class: [ProphetNetForCausalLM](model_doc/prophetnet.html#transformers.ProphetNetForCausalLM) (ProphetNet model)
  - [ReformerConfig](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerConfig) configuration class: [ReformerModelWithLMHead](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerModelWithLMHead) (Reformer model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [RemBertForCausalLM](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertForCausalLM) (RemBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [RoFormerForCausalLM](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerForCausalLM) (RoFormer model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [RobertaForCausalLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForCausalLM) (RoBERTa model)
  - [Speech2Text2Config](model_doc/speech_to_text_2.html#transformers.Speech2Text2Config) configuration class: [Speech2Text2ForCausalLM](model_doc/speech_to_text_2.html#transformers.Speech2Text2ForCausalLM) (Speech2Text2 model)
  - [TransfoXLConfig](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLConfig) configuration class: [TransfoXLLMHeadModel](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLLMHeadModel) (Transformer-XL model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [XLMWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMWithLMHeadModel) (XLM model)
  - [XLMProphetNetConfig](model_doc/xlmprophetnet.html#transformers.XLMProphetNetConfig) configuration class: [XLMProphetNetForCausalLM](model_doc/xlmprophetnet.html#transformers.XLMProphetNetForCausalLM) (XLMProphetNet model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [XLMRobertaForCausalLM](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForCausalLM) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [XLNetLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetLMHeadModel) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForCausalLM
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a causal language modeling head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **bart** -- [BartForCausalLM](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartForCausalLM) (BART model)
- **bert** -- [BertLMHeadModel](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertLMHeadModel) (BERT model)
- **bert-generation** -- [BertGenerationDecoder](model_doc/bertgeneration.html#transformers.BertGenerationDecoder) (Bert Generation model)
- **big_bird** -- [BigBirdForCausalLM](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForCausalLM) (BigBird model)
- **bigbird_pegasus** -- [BigBirdPegasusForCausalLM](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusForCausalLM) (BigBirdPegasus model)
- **blenderbot** -- [BlenderbotForCausalLM](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.BlenderbotForCausalLM) (Blenderbot model)
- **blenderbot-small** -- [BlenderbotSmallForCausalLM](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.BlenderbotSmallForCausalLM) (BlenderbotSmall model)
- **camembert** -- [CamembertForCausalLM](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForCausalLM) (CamemBERT model)
- **ctrl** -- [CTRLLMHeadModel](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLLMHeadModel) (CTRL model)
- **gpt2** -- [GPT2LMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2LMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
- **gpt_neo** -- [GPTNeoForCausalLM](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.GPTNeoForCausalLM) (GPT Neo model)
- **gptj** -- [GPTJForCausalLM](model_doc/gptj.html#transformers.GPTJForCausalLM) (GPT-J model)
- **marian** -- [MarianForCausalLM](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianForCausalLM) (Marian model)
- **mbart** -- [MBartForCausalLM](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartForCausalLM) (mBART model)
- **megatron-bert** -- [MegatronBertForCausalLM](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForCausalLM) (MegatronBert model)
- **openai-gpt** -- [OpenAIGPTLMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTLMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT model)
- **pegasus** -- [PegasusForCausalLM](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusForCausalLM) (Pegasus model)
- **prophetnet** -- [ProphetNetForCausalLM](model_doc/prophetnet.html#transformers.ProphetNetForCausalLM) (ProphetNet model)
- **reformer** -- [ReformerModelWithLMHead](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerModelWithLMHead) (Reformer model)
- **rembert** -- [RemBertForCausalLM](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertForCausalLM) (RemBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [RobertaForCausalLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForCausalLM) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [RoFormerForCausalLM](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerForCausalLM) (RoFormer model)
- **speech_to_text_2** -- [Speech2Text2ForCausalLM](model_doc/speech_to_text_2.html#transformers.Speech2Text2ForCausalLM) (Speech2Text2 model)
- **transfo-xl** -- [TransfoXLLMHeadModel](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLLMHeadModel) (Transformer-XL model)
- **xlm** -- [XLMWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMWithLMHeadModel) (XLM model)
- **xlm-prophetnet** -- [XLMProphetNetForCausalLM](model_doc/xlmprophetnet.html#transformers.XLMProphetNetForCausalLM) (XLMProphetNet model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [XLMRobertaForCausalLM](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForCausalLM) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [XLNetLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetLMHeadModel) (XLNet model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForCausalLM

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```


## AutoModelForMaskedLM

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForMaskedLM'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForMaskedLM**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a masked language modeling head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a masked language modeling head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [AlbertForMaskedLM](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertForMaskedLM) (ALBERT model)
  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [BartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [BertForMaskedLM](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForMaskedLM) (BERT model)
  - [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) configuration class: [BigBirdForMaskedLM](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForMaskedLM) (BigBird model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [CamembertForMaskedLM](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForMaskedLM) (CamemBERT model)
  - [ConvBertConfig](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertConfig) configuration class: [ConvBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertForMaskedLM) (ConvBERT model)
  - [DebertaConfig](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaConfig) configuration class: [DebertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaForMaskedLM) (DeBERTa model)
  - [DebertaV2Config](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Config) configuration class: [DebertaV2ForMaskedLM](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2ForMaskedLM) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [DistilBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertForMaskedLM) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [ElectraForMaskedLM](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraForMaskedLM) (ELECTRA model)
  - [FNetConfig](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetConfig) configuration class: [FNetForMaskedLM](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForMaskedLM) (FNet model)
  - [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) configuration class: [FlaubertWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertWithLMHeadModel) (FlauBERT model)
  - [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) configuration class: [FunnelForMaskedLM](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelForMaskedLM) (Funnel Transformer model)
  - [IBertConfig](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertConfig) configuration class: [IBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertForMaskedLM) (I-BERT model)
  - [LayoutLMConfig](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMConfig) configuration class: [LayoutLMForMaskedLM](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMForMaskedLM) (LayoutLM model)
  - [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) configuration class: [LongformerForMaskedLM](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerForMaskedLM) (Longformer model)
  - [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) configuration class: [MBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartForConditionalGeneration) (mBART model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [MPNetForMaskedLM](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetForMaskedLM) (MPNet model)
  - [MegatronBertConfig](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertConfig) configuration class: [MegatronBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForMaskedLM) (MegatronBert model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [MobileBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForMaskedLM) (MobileBERT model)
  - [ReformerConfig](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerConfig) configuration class: [ReformerForMaskedLM](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerForMaskedLM) (Reformer model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [RemBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertForMaskedLM) (RemBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [RoFormerForMaskedLM](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerForMaskedLM) (RoFormer model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [RobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForMaskedLM) (RoBERTa model)
  - [SqueezeBertConfig](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertConfig) configuration class: [SqueezeBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertForMaskedLM) (SqueezeBERT model)
  - [TapasConfig](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasConfig) configuration class: [TapasForMaskedLM](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasForMaskedLM) (TAPAS model)
  - [Wav2Vec2Config](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2Config) configuration class: `Wav2Vec2ForMaskedLM` (Wav2Vec2 model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [XLMWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMWithLMHeadModel) (XLM model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [XLMRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForMaskedLM) (XLM-RoBERTa model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForMaskedLM
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = AutoModelForMaskedLM.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a masked language modeling head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [AlbertForMaskedLM](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertForMaskedLM) (ALBERT model)
- **bart** -- [BartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
- **bert** -- [BertForMaskedLM](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForMaskedLM) (BERT model)
- **big_bird** -- [BigBirdForMaskedLM](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForMaskedLM) (BigBird model)
- **camembert** -- [CamembertForMaskedLM](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForMaskedLM) (CamemBERT model)
- **convbert** -- [ConvBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertForMaskedLM) (ConvBERT model)
- **deberta** -- [DebertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaForMaskedLM) (DeBERTa model)
- **deberta-v2** -- [DebertaV2ForMaskedLM](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2ForMaskedLM) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
- **distilbert** -- [DistilBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertForMaskedLM) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [ElectraForMaskedLM](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraForMaskedLM) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [FlaubertWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertWithLMHeadModel) (FlauBERT model)
- **fnet** -- [FNetForMaskedLM](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForMaskedLM) (FNet model)
- **funnel** -- [FunnelForMaskedLM](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelForMaskedLM) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **ibert** -- [IBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertForMaskedLM) (I-BERT model)
- **layoutlm** -- [LayoutLMForMaskedLM](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMForMaskedLM) (LayoutLM model)
- **longformer** -- [LongformerForMaskedLM](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerForMaskedLM) (Longformer model)
- **mbart** -- [MBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartForConditionalGeneration) (mBART model)
- **megatron-bert** -- [MegatronBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForMaskedLM) (MegatronBert model)
- **mobilebert** -- [MobileBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForMaskedLM) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [MPNetForMaskedLM](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetForMaskedLM) (MPNet model)
- **reformer** -- [ReformerForMaskedLM](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerForMaskedLM) (Reformer model)
- **rembert** -- [RemBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertForMaskedLM) (RemBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [RobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForMaskedLM) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [RoFormerForMaskedLM](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerForMaskedLM) (RoFormer model)
- **squeezebert** -- [SqueezeBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertForMaskedLM) (SqueezeBERT model)
- **tapas** -- [TapasForMaskedLM](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasForMaskedLM) (TAPAS model)
- **wav2vec2** -- `Wav2Vec2ForMaskedLM` (Wav2Vec2 model)
- **xlm** -- [XLMWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMWithLMHeadModel) (XLM model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [XLMRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForMaskedLM) (XLM-RoBERTa model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForMaskedLM

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForMaskedLM.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForMaskedLM.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModelForMaskedLM.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```


## AutoModelForSeq2SeqLM

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForSeq2SeqLM'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForSeq2SeqLM**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence-to-sequence language modeling head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence-to-sequence language modeling head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [BartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
  - [BigBirdPegasusConfig](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusConfig) configuration class: [BigBirdPegasusForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusForConditionalGeneration) (BigBirdPegasus model)
  - [BlenderbotConfig](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.BlenderbotConfig) configuration class: [BlenderbotForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.BlenderbotForConditionalGeneration) (Blenderbot model)
  - [BlenderbotSmallConfig](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.BlenderbotSmallConfig) configuration class: [BlenderbotSmallForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.BlenderbotSmallForConditionalGeneration) (BlenderbotSmall model)
  - [EncoderDecoderConfig](model_doc/encoderdecoder.html#transformers.EncoderDecoderConfig) configuration class: [EncoderDecoderModel](model_doc/encoderdecoder.html#transformers.EncoderDecoderModel) (Encoder decoder model)
  - [FSMTConfig](model_doc/fsmt.html#transformers.FSMTConfig) configuration class: [FSMTForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/fsmt.html#transformers.FSMTForConditionalGeneration) (FairSeq Machine-Translation model)
  - [LEDConfig](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDConfig) configuration class: [LEDForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDForConditionalGeneration) (LED model)
  - [M2M100Config](model_doc/m2m_100.html#transformers.M2M100Config) configuration class: [M2M100ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/m2m_100.html#transformers.M2M100ForConditionalGeneration) (M2M100 model)
  - [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) configuration class: [MBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartForConditionalGeneration) (mBART model)
  - [MT5Config](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.MT5Config) configuration class: [MT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.MT5ForConditionalGeneration) (mT5 model)
  - [MarianConfig](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianConfig) configuration class: [MarianMTModel](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianMTModel) (Marian model)
  - [PegasusConfig](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusConfig) configuration class: [PegasusForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusForConditionalGeneration) (Pegasus model)
  - [ProphetNetConfig](model_doc/prophetnet.html#transformers.ProphetNetConfig) configuration class: [ProphetNetForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/prophetnet.html#transformers.ProphetNetForConditionalGeneration) (ProphetNet model)
  - [T5Config](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Config) configuration class: [T5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5ForConditionalGeneration) (T5 model)
  - [XLMProphetNetConfig](model_doc/xlmprophetnet.html#transformers.XLMProphetNetConfig) configuration class: [XLMProphetNetForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/xlmprophetnet.html#transformers.XLMProphetNetForConditionalGeneration) (XLMProphetNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForSeq2SeqLM
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('t5-base')
>>> model = AutoModelForSeq2SeqLM.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence-to-sequence language modeling head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **bart** -- [BartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
- **bigbird_pegasus** -- [BigBirdPegasusForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusForConditionalGeneration) (BigBirdPegasus model)
- **blenderbot** -- [BlenderbotForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.BlenderbotForConditionalGeneration) (Blenderbot model)
- **blenderbot-small** -- [BlenderbotSmallForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.BlenderbotSmallForConditionalGeneration) (BlenderbotSmall model)
- **encoder-decoder** -- [EncoderDecoderModel](model_doc/encoderdecoder.html#transformers.EncoderDecoderModel) (Encoder decoder model)
- **fsmt** -- [FSMTForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/fsmt.html#transformers.FSMTForConditionalGeneration) (FairSeq Machine-Translation model)
- **led** -- [LEDForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDForConditionalGeneration) (LED model)
- **m2m_100** -- [M2M100ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/m2m_100.html#transformers.M2M100ForConditionalGeneration) (M2M100 model)
- **marian** -- [MarianMTModel](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianMTModel) (Marian model)
- **mbart** -- [MBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartForConditionalGeneration) (mBART model)
- **mt5** -- [MT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.MT5ForConditionalGeneration) (mT5 model)
- **pegasus** -- [PegasusForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusForConditionalGeneration) (Pegasus model)
- **prophetnet** -- [ProphetNetForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/prophetnet.html#transformers.ProphetNetForConditionalGeneration) (ProphetNet model)
- **t5** -- [T5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5ForConditionalGeneration) (T5 model)
- **xlm-prophetnet** -- [XLMProphetNetForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/xlmprophetnet.html#transformers.XLMProphetNetForConditionalGeneration) (XLMProphetNet model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForSeq2SeqLM

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForSeq2SeqLM.from_pretrained('t5-base')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForSeq2SeqLM.from_pretrained('t5-base', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/t5_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModelForSeq2SeqLM.from_pretrained('./tf_model/t5_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```


## AutoModelForSequenceClassification

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForSequenceClassification'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForSequenceClassification**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence classification head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence classification head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [AlbertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertForSequenceClassification) (ALBERT model)
  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [BartForSequenceClassification](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartForSequenceClassification) (BART model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [BertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForSequenceClassification) (BERT model)
  - [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) configuration class: [BigBirdForSequenceClassification](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForSequenceClassification) (BigBird model)
  - [BigBirdPegasusConfig](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusConfig) configuration class: [BigBirdPegasusForSequenceClassification](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusForSequenceClassification) (BigBirdPegasus model)
  - [CTRLConfig](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLConfig) configuration class: [CTRLForSequenceClassification](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLForSequenceClassification) (CTRL model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [CamembertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForSequenceClassification) (CamemBERT model)
  - [CanineConfig](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineConfig) configuration class: [CanineForSequenceClassification](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineForSequenceClassification) (Canine model)
  - [ConvBertConfig](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertConfig) configuration class: [ConvBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertForSequenceClassification) (ConvBERT model)
  - [DebertaConfig](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaConfig) configuration class: [DebertaForSequenceClassification](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaForSequenceClassification) (DeBERTa model)
  - [DebertaV2Config](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Config) configuration class: [DebertaV2ForSequenceClassification](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2ForSequenceClassification) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [DistilBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertForSequenceClassification) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [ElectraForSequenceClassification](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraForSequenceClassification) (ELECTRA model)
  - [FNetConfig](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetConfig) configuration class: [FNetForSequenceClassification](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForSequenceClassification) (FNet model)
  - [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) configuration class: [FlaubertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertForSequenceClassification) (FlauBERT model)
  - [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) configuration class: [FunnelForSequenceClassification](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelForSequenceClassification) (Funnel Transformer model)
  - [GPT2Config](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Config) configuration class: [GPT2ForSequenceClassification](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2ForSequenceClassification) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
  - [GPTJConfig](model_doc/gptj.html#transformers.GPTJConfig) configuration class: [GPTJForSequenceClassification](model_doc/gptj.html#transformers.GPTJForSequenceClassification) (GPT-J model)
  - [GPTNeoConfig](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.GPTNeoConfig) configuration class: [GPTNeoForSequenceClassification](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.GPTNeoForSequenceClassification) (GPT Neo model)
  - [IBertConfig](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertConfig) configuration class: [IBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertForSequenceClassification) (I-BERT model)
  - [LEDConfig](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDConfig) configuration class: [LEDForSequenceClassification](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDForSequenceClassification) (LED model)
  - [LayoutLMConfig](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMConfig) configuration class: [LayoutLMForSequenceClassification](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMForSequenceClassification) (LayoutLM model)
  - [LayoutLMv2Config](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2Config) configuration class: [LayoutLMv2ForSequenceClassification](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2ForSequenceClassification) (LayoutLMv2 model)
  - [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) configuration class: [LongformerForSequenceClassification](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerForSequenceClassification) (Longformer model)
  - [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) configuration class: [MBartForSequenceClassification](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartForSequenceClassification) (mBART model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [MPNetForSequenceClassification](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetForSequenceClassification) (MPNet model)
  - [MegatronBertConfig](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertConfig) configuration class: [MegatronBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForSequenceClassification) (MegatronBert model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [MobileBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForSequenceClassification) (MobileBERT model)
  - [OpenAIGPTConfig](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTConfig) configuration class: [OpenAIGPTForSequenceClassification](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTForSequenceClassification) (OpenAI GPT model)
  - [ReformerConfig](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerConfig) configuration class: [ReformerForSequenceClassification](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerForSequenceClassification) (Reformer model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [RemBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertForSequenceClassification) (RemBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [RoFormerForSequenceClassification](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerForSequenceClassification) (RoFormer model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [RobertaForSequenceClassification](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForSequenceClassification) (RoBERTa model)
  - [SqueezeBertConfig](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertConfig) configuration class: [SqueezeBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertForSequenceClassification) (SqueezeBERT model)
  - [TapasConfig](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasConfig) configuration class: [TapasForSequenceClassification](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasForSequenceClassification) (TAPAS model)
  - [TransfoXLConfig](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLConfig) configuration class: [TransfoXLForSequenceClassification](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLForSequenceClassification) (Transformer-XL model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [XLMForSequenceClassification](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMForSequenceClassification) (XLM model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [XLMRobertaForSequenceClassification](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForSequenceClassification) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [XLNetForSequenceClassification](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetForSequenceClassification) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForSequenceClassification
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = AutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence classification head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [AlbertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertForSequenceClassification) (ALBERT model)
- **bart** -- [BartForSequenceClassification](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartForSequenceClassification) (BART model)
- **bert** -- [BertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForSequenceClassification) (BERT model)
- **big_bird** -- [BigBirdForSequenceClassification](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForSequenceClassification) (BigBird model)
- **bigbird_pegasus** -- [BigBirdPegasusForSequenceClassification](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusForSequenceClassification) (BigBirdPegasus model)
- **camembert** -- [CamembertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForSequenceClassification) (CamemBERT model)
- **canine** -- [CanineForSequenceClassification](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineForSequenceClassification) (Canine model)
- **convbert** -- [ConvBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertForSequenceClassification) (ConvBERT model)
- **ctrl** -- [CTRLForSequenceClassification](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLForSequenceClassification) (CTRL model)
- **deberta** -- [DebertaForSequenceClassification](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaForSequenceClassification) (DeBERTa model)
- **deberta-v2** -- [DebertaV2ForSequenceClassification](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2ForSequenceClassification) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
- **distilbert** -- [DistilBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertForSequenceClassification) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [ElectraForSequenceClassification](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraForSequenceClassification) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [FlaubertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertForSequenceClassification) (FlauBERT model)
- **fnet** -- [FNetForSequenceClassification](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForSequenceClassification) (FNet model)
- **funnel** -- [FunnelForSequenceClassification](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelForSequenceClassification) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **gpt2** -- [GPT2ForSequenceClassification](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2ForSequenceClassification) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
- **gpt_neo** -- [GPTNeoForSequenceClassification](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.GPTNeoForSequenceClassification) (GPT Neo model)
- **gptj** -- [GPTJForSequenceClassification](model_doc/gptj.html#transformers.GPTJForSequenceClassification) (GPT-J model)
- **ibert** -- [IBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertForSequenceClassification) (I-BERT model)
- **layoutlm** -- [LayoutLMForSequenceClassification](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMForSequenceClassification) (LayoutLM model)
- **layoutlmv2** -- [LayoutLMv2ForSequenceClassification](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2ForSequenceClassification) (LayoutLMv2 model)
- **led** -- [LEDForSequenceClassification](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDForSequenceClassification) (LED model)
- **longformer** -- [LongformerForSequenceClassification](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerForSequenceClassification) (Longformer model)
- **mbart** -- [MBartForSequenceClassification](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartForSequenceClassification) (mBART model)
- **megatron-bert** -- [MegatronBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForSequenceClassification) (MegatronBert model)
- **mobilebert** -- [MobileBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForSequenceClassification) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [MPNetForSequenceClassification](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetForSequenceClassification) (MPNet model)
- **openai-gpt** -- [OpenAIGPTForSequenceClassification](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTForSequenceClassification) (OpenAI GPT model)
- **reformer** -- [ReformerForSequenceClassification](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerForSequenceClassification) (Reformer model)
- **rembert** -- [RemBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertForSequenceClassification) (RemBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [RobertaForSequenceClassification](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForSequenceClassification) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [RoFormerForSequenceClassification](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerForSequenceClassification) (RoFormer model)
- **squeezebert** -- [SqueezeBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertForSequenceClassification) (SqueezeBERT model)
- **tapas** -- [TapasForSequenceClassification](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasForSequenceClassification) (TAPAS model)
- **transfo-xl** -- [TransfoXLForSequenceClassification](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLForSequenceClassification) (Transformer-XL model)
- **xlm** -- [XLMForSequenceClassification](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMForSequenceClassification) (XLM model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [XLMRobertaForSequenceClassification](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForSequenceClassification) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [XLNetForSequenceClassification](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetForSequenceClassification) (XLNet model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForSequenceClassification

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```


## AutoModelForMultipleChoice

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForMultipleChoice'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForMultipleChoice**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a multiple choice head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a multiple choice head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [AlbertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertForMultipleChoice) (ALBERT model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [BertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForMultipleChoice) (BERT model)
  - [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) configuration class: [BigBirdForMultipleChoice](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForMultipleChoice) (BigBird model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [CamembertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForMultipleChoice) (CamemBERT model)
  - [CanineConfig](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineConfig) configuration class: [CanineForMultipleChoice](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineForMultipleChoice) (Canine model)
  - [ConvBertConfig](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertConfig) configuration class: [ConvBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertForMultipleChoice) (ConvBERT model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [DistilBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertForMultipleChoice) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [ElectraForMultipleChoice](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraForMultipleChoice) (ELECTRA model)
  - [FNetConfig](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetConfig) configuration class: [FNetForMultipleChoice](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForMultipleChoice) (FNet model)
  - [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) configuration class: [FlaubertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertForMultipleChoice) (FlauBERT model)
  - [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) configuration class: [FunnelForMultipleChoice](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelForMultipleChoice) (Funnel Transformer model)
  - [IBertConfig](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertConfig) configuration class: [IBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertForMultipleChoice) (I-BERT model)
  - [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) configuration class: [LongformerForMultipleChoice](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerForMultipleChoice) (Longformer model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [MPNetForMultipleChoice](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetForMultipleChoice) (MPNet model)
  - [MegatronBertConfig](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertConfig) configuration class: [MegatronBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForMultipleChoice) (MegatronBert model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [MobileBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForMultipleChoice) (MobileBERT model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [RemBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertForMultipleChoice) (RemBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [RoFormerForMultipleChoice](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerForMultipleChoice) (RoFormer model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [RobertaForMultipleChoice](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForMultipleChoice) (RoBERTa model)
  - [SqueezeBertConfig](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertConfig) configuration class: [SqueezeBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertForMultipleChoice) (SqueezeBERT model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [XLMForMultipleChoice](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMForMultipleChoice) (XLM model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [XLMRobertaForMultipleChoice](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForMultipleChoice) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [XLNetForMultipleChoice](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetForMultipleChoice) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForMultipleChoice
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = AutoModelForMultipleChoice.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a multiple choice head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [AlbertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertForMultipleChoice) (ALBERT model)
- **bert** -- [BertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForMultipleChoice) (BERT model)
- **big_bird** -- [BigBirdForMultipleChoice](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForMultipleChoice) (BigBird model)
- **camembert** -- [CamembertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForMultipleChoice) (CamemBERT model)
- **canine** -- [CanineForMultipleChoice](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineForMultipleChoice) (Canine model)
- **convbert** -- [ConvBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertForMultipleChoice) (ConvBERT model)
- **distilbert** -- [DistilBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertForMultipleChoice) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [ElectraForMultipleChoice](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraForMultipleChoice) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [FlaubertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertForMultipleChoice) (FlauBERT model)
- **fnet** -- [FNetForMultipleChoice](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForMultipleChoice) (FNet model)
- **funnel** -- [FunnelForMultipleChoice](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelForMultipleChoice) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **ibert** -- [IBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertForMultipleChoice) (I-BERT model)
- **longformer** -- [LongformerForMultipleChoice](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerForMultipleChoice) (Longformer model)
- **megatron-bert** -- [MegatronBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForMultipleChoice) (MegatronBert model)
- **mobilebert** -- [MobileBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForMultipleChoice) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [MPNetForMultipleChoice](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetForMultipleChoice) (MPNet model)
- **rembert** -- [RemBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertForMultipleChoice) (RemBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [RobertaForMultipleChoice](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForMultipleChoice) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [RoFormerForMultipleChoice](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerForMultipleChoice) (RoFormer model)
- **squeezebert** -- [SqueezeBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertForMultipleChoice) (SqueezeBERT model)
- **xlm** -- [XLMForMultipleChoice](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMForMultipleChoice) (XLM model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [XLMRobertaForMultipleChoice](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForMultipleChoice) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [XLNetForMultipleChoice](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetForMultipleChoice) (XLNet model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
