    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForMultipleChoice

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForMultipleChoice.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForMultipleChoice.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModelForMultipleChoice.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```


## AutoModelForNextSentencePrediction

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForNextSentencePrediction'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForNextSentencePrediction**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a next sentence prediction head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a next sentence prediction head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [BertForNextSentencePrediction](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForNextSentencePrediction) (BERT model)
  - [FNetConfig](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetConfig) configuration class: [FNetForNextSentencePrediction](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForNextSentencePrediction) (FNet model)
  - [MegatronBertConfig](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertConfig) configuration class: [MegatronBertForNextSentencePrediction](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForNextSentencePrediction) (MegatronBert model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [MobileBertForNextSentencePrediction](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForNextSentencePrediction) (MobileBERT model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForNextSentencePrediction
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = AutoModelForNextSentencePrediction.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a next sentence prediction head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **bert** -- [BertForNextSentencePrediction](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForNextSentencePrediction) (BERT model)
- **fnet** -- [FNetForNextSentencePrediction](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForNextSentencePrediction) (FNet model)
- **megatron-bert** -- [MegatronBertForNextSentencePrediction](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForNextSentencePrediction) (MegatronBert model)
- **mobilebert** -- [MobileBertForNextSentencePrediction](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForNextSentencePrediction) (MobileBERT model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForNextSentencePrediction

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForNextSentencePrediction.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForNextSentencePrediction.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModelForNextSentencePrediction.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```


## AutoModelForTokenClassification

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForTokenClassification'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForTokenClassification**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a token classification head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a token classification head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [AlbertForTokenClassification](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertForTokenClassification) (ALBERT model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [BertForTokenClassification](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForTokenClassification) (BERT model)
  - [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) configuration class: [BigBirdForTokenClassification](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForTokenClassification) (BigBird model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [CamembertForTokenClassification](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForTokenClassification) (CamemBERT model)
  - [CanineConfig](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineConfig) configuration class: [CanineForTokenClassification](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineForTokenClassification) (Canine model)
  - [ConvBertConfig](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertConfig) configuration class: [ConvBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertForTokenClassification) (ConvBERT model)
  - [DebertaConfig](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaConfig) configuration class: [DebertaForTokenClassification](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaForTokenClassification) (DeBERTa model)
  - [DebertaV2Config](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Config) configuration class: [DebertaV2ForTokenClassification](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2ForTokenClassification) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [DistilBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertForTokenClassification) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [ElectraForTokenClassification](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraForTokenClassification) (ELECTRA model)
  - [FNetConfig](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetConfig) configuration class: [FNetForTokenClassification](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForTokenClassification) (FNet model)
  - [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) configuration class: [FlaubertForTokenClassification](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertForTokenClassification) (FlauBERT model)
  - [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) configuration class: [FunnelForTokenClassification](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelForTokenClassification) (Funnel Transformer model)
  - [GPT2Config](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Config) configuration class: [GPT2ForTokenClassification](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2ForTokenClassification) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
  - [IBertConfig](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertConfig) configuration class: [IBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertForTokenClassification) (I-BERT model)
  - [LayoutLMConfig](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMConfig) configuration class: [LayoutLMForTokenClassification](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMForTokenClassification) (LayoutLM model)
  - [LayoutLMv2Config](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2Config) configuration class: [LayoutLMv2ForTokenClassification](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2ForTokenClassification) (LayoutLMv2 model)
  - [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) configuration class: [LongformerForTokenClassification](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerForTokenClassification) (Longformer model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [MPNetForTokenClassification](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetForTokenClassification) (MPNet model)
  - [MegatronBertConfig](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertConfig) configuration class: [MegatronBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForTokenClassification) (MegatronBert model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [MobileBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForTokenClassification) (MobileBERT model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [RemBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertForTokenClassification) (RemBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [RoFormerForTokenClassification](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerForTokenClassification) (RoFormer model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [RobertaForTokenClassification](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForTokenClassification) (RoBERTa model)
  - [SqueezeBertConfig](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertConfig) configuration class: [SqueezeBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertForTokenClassification) (SqueezeBERT model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [XLMForTokenClassification](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMForTokenClassification) (XLM model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [XLMRobertaForTokenClassification](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForTokenClassification) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [XLNetForTokenClassification](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetForTokenClassification) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForTokenClassification
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = AutoModelForTokenClassification.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a token classification head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [AlbertForTokenClassification](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertForTokenClassification) (ALBERT model)
- **bert** -- [BertForTokenClassification](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForTokenClassification) (BERT model)
- **big_bird** -- [BigBirdForTokenClassification](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForTokenClassification) (BigBird model)
- **camembert** -- [CamembertForTokenClassification](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForTokenClassification) (CamemBERT model)
- **canine** -- [CanineForTokenClassification](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineForTokenClassification) (Canine model)
- **convbert** -- [ConvBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertForTokenClassification) (ConvBERT model)
- **deberta** -- [DebertaForTokenClassification](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaForTokenClassification) (DeBERTa model)
- **deberta-v2** -- [DebertaV2ForTokenClassification](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2ForTokenClassification) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
- **distilbert** -- [DistilBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertForTokenClassification) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [ElectraForTokenClassification](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraForTokenClassification) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [FlaubertForTokenClassification](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertForTokenClassification) (FlauBERT model)
- **fnet** -- [FNetForTokenClassification](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForTokenClassification) (FNet model)
- **funnel** -- [FunnelForTokenClassification](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelForTokenClassification) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **gpt2** -- [GPT2ForTokenClassification](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2ForTokenClassification) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
- **ibert** -- [IBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertForTokenClassification) (I-BERT model)
- **layoutlm** -- [LayoutLMForTokenClassification](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMForTokenClassification) (LayoutLM model)
- **layoutlmv2** -- [LayoutLMv2ForTokenClassification](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2ForTokenClassification) (LayoutLMv2 model)
- **longformer** -- [LongformerForTokenClassification](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerForTokenClassification) (Longformer model)
- **megatron-bert** -- [MegatronBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForTokenClassification) (MegatronBert model)
- **mobilebert** -- [MobileBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForTokenClassification) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [MPNetForTokenClassification](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetForTokenClassification) (MPNet model)
- **rembert** -- [RemBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertForTokenClassification) (RemBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [RobertaForTokenClassification](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForTokenClassification) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [RoFormerForTokenClassification](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerForTokenClassification) (RoFormer model)
- **squeezebert** -- [SqueezeBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertForTokenClassification) (SqueezeBERT model)
- **xlm** -- [XLMForTokenClassification](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMForTokenClassification) (XLM model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [XLMRobertaForTokenClassification](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForTokenClassification) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [XLNetForTokenClassification](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetForTokenClassification) (XLNet model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForTokenClassification

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForTokenClassification.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForTokenClassification.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModelForTokenClassification.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```


## AutoModelForQuestionAnswering

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForQuestionAnswering'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForQuestionAnswering**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a question answering head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a question answering head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [AlbertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertForQuestionAnswering) (ALBERT model)
  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [BartForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartForQuestionAnswering) (BART model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [BertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForQuestionAnswering) (BERT model)
  - [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) configuration class: [BigBirdForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForQuestionAnswering) (BigBird model)
  - [BigBirdPegasusConfig](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusConfig) configuration class: [BigBirdPegasusForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusForQuestionAnswering) (BigBirdPegasus model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [CamembertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForQuestionAnswering) (CamemBERT model)
  - [CanineConfig](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineConfig) configuration class: [CanineForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineForQuestionAnswering) (Canine model)
  - [ConvBertConfig](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertConfig) configuration class: [ConvBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertForQuestionAnswering) (ConvBERT model)
  - [DebertaConfig](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaConfig) configuration class: [DebertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaForQuestionAnswering) (DeBERTa model)
  - [DebertaV2Config](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Config) configuration class: [DebertaV2ForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2ForQuestionAnswering) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [DistilBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertForQuestionAnswering) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [ElectraForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraForQuestionAnswering) (ELECTRA model)
  - [FNetConfig](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetConfig) configuration class: [FNetForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForQuestionAnswering) (FNet model)
  - [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) configuration class: [FlaubertForQuestionAnsweringSimple](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertForQuestionAnsweringSimple) (FlauBERT model)
  - [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) configuration class: [FunnelForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelForQuestionAnswering) (Funnel Transformer model)
  - [IBertConfig](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertConfig) configuration class: [IBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertForQuestionAnswering) (I-BERT model)
  - [LEDConfig](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDConfig) configuration class: [LEDForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDForQuestionAnswering) (LED model)
  - [LayoutLMv2Config](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2Config) configuration class: [LayoutLMv2ForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2ForQuestionAnswering) (LayoutLMv2 model)
  - [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) configuration class: [LongformerForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerForQuestionAnswering) (Longformer model)
  - [LxmertConfig](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertConfig) configuration class: [LxmertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertForQuestionAnswering) (LXMERT model)
  - [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) configuration class: [MBartForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartForQuestionAnswering) (mBART model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [MPNetForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetForQuestionAnswering) (MPNet model)
  - [MegatronBertConfig](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertConfig) configuration class: [MegatronBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForQuestionAnswering) (MegatronBert model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [MobileBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForQuestionAnswering) (MobileBERT model)
  - [ReformerConfig](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerConfig) configuration class: [ReformerForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerForQuestionAnswering) (Reformer model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [RemBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertForQuestionAnswering) (RemBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [RoFormerForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerForQuestionAnswering) (RoFormer model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [RobertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForQuestionAnswering) (RoBERTa model)
  - [SplinterConfig](model_doc/splinter.html#transformers.SplinterConfig) configuration class: [SplinterForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/splinter.html#transformers.SplinterForQuestionAnswering) (Splinter model)
  - [SqueezeBertConfig](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertConfig) configuration class: [SqueezeBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertForQuestionAnswering) (SqueezeBERT model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [XLMForQuestionAnsweringSimple](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMForQuestionAnsweringSimple) (XLM model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [XLMRobertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForQuestionAnswering) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [XLNetForQuestionAnsweringSimple](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetForQuestionAnsweringSimple) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForQuestionAnswering
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = AutoModelForQuestionAnswering.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a question answering head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [AlbertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertForQuestionAnswering) (ALBERT model)
- **bart** -- [BartForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartForQuestionAnswering) (BART model)
- **bert** -- [BertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertForQuestionAnswering) (BERT model)
- **big_bird** -- [BigBirdForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdForQuestionAnswering) (BigBird model)
- **bigbird_pegasus** -- [BigBirdPegasusForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bigbird_pegasus.html#transformers.BigBirdPegasusForQuestionAnswering) (BigBirdPegasus model)
- **camembert** -- [CamembertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertForQuestionAnswering) (CamemBERT model)
- **canine** -- [CanineForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/canine.html#transformers.CanineForQuestionAnswering) (Canine model)
- **convbert** -- [ConvBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertForQuestionAnswering) (ConvBERT model)
- **deberta** -- [DebertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaForQuestionAnswering) (DeBERTa model)
- **deberta-v2** -- [DebertaV2ForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2ForQuestionAnswering) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
- **distilbert** -- [DistilBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertForQuestionAnswering) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [ElectraForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraForQuestionAnswering) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [FlaubertForQuestionAnsweringSimple](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertForQuestionAnsweringSimple) (FlauBERT model)
- **fnet** -- [FNetForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/fnet.html#transformers.FNetForQuestionAnswering) (FNet model)
- **funnel** -- [FunnelForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelForQuestionAnswering) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **ibert** -- [IBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/ibert.html#transformers.IBertForQuestionAnswering) (I-BERT model)
- **layoutlmv2** -- [LayoutLMv2ForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/layoutlmv2.html#transformers.LayoutLMv2ForQuestionAnswering) (LayoutLMv2 model)
- **led** -- [LEDForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDForQuestionAnswering) (LED model)
- **longformer** -- [LongformerForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerForQuestionAnswering) (Longformer model)
- **lxmert** -- [LxmertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertForQuestionAnswering) (LXMERT model)
- **mbart** -- [MBartForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartForQuestionAnswering) (mBART model)
- **megatron-bert** -- [MegatronBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/megatron_bert.html#transformers.MegatronBertForQuestionAnswering) (MegatronBert model)
- **mobilebert** -- [MobileBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertForQuestionAnswering) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [MPNetForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetForQuestionAnswering) (MPNet model)
- **reformer** -- [ReformerForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/reformer.html#transformers.ReformerForQuestionAnswering) (Reformer model)
- **rembert** -- [RemBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertForQuestionAnswering) (RemBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [RobertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaForQuestionAnswering) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [RoFormerForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerForQuestionAnswering) (RoFormer model)
- **splinter** -- [SplinterForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/splinter.html#transformers.SplinterForQuestionAnswering) (Splinter model)
- **squeezebert** -- [SqueezeBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/squeezebert.html#transformers.SqueezeBertForQuestionAnswering) (SqueezeBERT model)
- **xlm** -- [XLMForQuestionAnsweringSimple](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMForQuestionAnsweringSimple) (XLM model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [XLMRobertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaForQuestionAnswering) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [XLNetForQuestionAnsweringSimple](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetForQuestionAnsweringSimple) (XLNet model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForQuestionAnswering

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForQuestionAnswering.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForQuestionAnswering.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModelForQuestionAnswering.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```


## AutoModelForTableQuestionAnswering

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForTableQuestionAnswering'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForTableQuestionAnswering**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a table question answering head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a table question answering head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [TapasConfig](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasConfig) configuration class: [TapasForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasForQuestionAnswering) (TAPAS model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForTableQuestionAnswering
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('google/tapas-base-finetuned-wtq')
>>> model = AutoModelForTableQuestionAnswering.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a table question answering head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **tapas** -- [TapasForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/tapas.html#transformers.TapasForQuestionAnswering) (TAPAS model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForTableQuestionAnswering

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForTableQuestionAnswering.from_pretrained('google/tapas-base-finetuned-wtq')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForTableQuestionAnswering.from_pretrained('google/tapas-base-finetuned-wtq', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/tapas_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModelForTableQuestionAnswering.from_pretrained('./tf_model/tapas_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```


## AutoModelForImageClassification

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForImageClassification'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForImageClassification**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a image classification head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a image classification head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [BeitConfig](model_doc/beit.html#transformers.BeitConfig) configuration class: [BeitForImageClassification](model_doc/beit.html#transformers.BeitForImageClassification) (BeiT model)
  - [DeiTConfig](model_doc/deit.html#transformers.DeiTConfig) configuration class: [DeiTForImageClassification](model_doc/deit.html#transformers.DeiTForImageClassification) or [DeiTForImageClassificationWithTeacher](model_doc/deit.html#transformers.DeiTForImageClassificationWithTeacher) (DeiT model)
  - [ViTConfig](model_doc/vit.html#transformers.ViTConfig) configuration class: [ViTForImageClassification](model_doc/vit.html#transformers.ViTForImageClassification) (ViT model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForImageClassification
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = AutoModelForImageClassification.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a image classification head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **beit** -- [BeitForImageClassification](model_doc/beit.html#transformers.BeitForImageClassification) (BeiT model)
- **deit** -- [DeiTForImageClassification](model_doc/deit.html#transformers.DeiTForImageClassification) or [DeiTForImageClassificationWithTeacher](model_doc/deit.html#transformers.DeiTForImageClassificationWithTeacher) (DeiT model)
- **vit** -- [ViTForImageClassification](model_doc/vit.html#transformers.ViTForImageClassification) (ViT model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForImageClassification

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForImageClassification.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForImageClassification.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModelForImageClassification.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```
