## AutoModelForCTC

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForCTC'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForCTC**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a connectionist temporal classification head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a connectionist temporal classification head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [HubertConfig](model_doc/hubert.html#transformers.HubertConfig) configuration class: [HubertForCTC](model_doc/hubert.html#transformers.HubertForCTC) (Hubert model)
  - [Wav2Vec2Config](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2Config) configuration class: [Wav2Vec2ForCTC](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2ForCTC) (Wav2Vec2 model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForCTC
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = AutoModelForCTC.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a connectionist temporal classification head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **hubert** -- [HubertForCTC](model_doc/hubert.html#transformers.HubertForCTC) (Hubert model)
- **wav2vec2** -- [Wav2Vec2ForCTC](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2ForCTC) (Wav2Vec2 model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForCTC

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForCTC.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForCTC.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModelForCTC.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```


## AutoModelForSpeechSeq2Seq

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForSpeechSeq2Seq'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForSpeechSeq2Seq**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence-to-sequence speech-to-text modeing head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence-to-sequence speech-to-text modeing head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [Speech2TextConfig](model_doc/speech_to_text.html#transformers.Speech2TextConfig) configuration class: [Speech2TextForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/speech_to_text.html#transformers.Speech2TextForConditionalGeneration) (Speech2Text model)
  - [SpeechEncoderDecoderConfig](model_doc/speechencoderdecoder.html#transformers.SpeechEncoderDecoderConfig) configuration class: [SpeechEncoderDecoderModel](model_doc/speechencoderdecoder.html#transformers.SpeechEncoderDecoderModel) (Speech Encoder decoder model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForSpeechSeq2Seq
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = AutoModelForSpeechSeq2Seq.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence-to-sequence speech-to-text modeing head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **speech-encoder-decoder** -- [SpeechEncoderDecoderModel](model_doc/speechencoderdecoder.html#transformers.SpeechEncoderDecoderModel) (Speech Encoder decoder model)
- **speech_to_text** -- [Speech2TextForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/speech_to_text.html#transformers.Speech2TextForConditionalGeneration) (Speech2Text model)

The model is set in evaluation mode by default using `model.eval()` (so for instance, dropout modules are
deactivated). To train the model, you should first set it back in training mode with `model.train()`

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _tensorflow index checkpoint file_ (e.g, `./tf_model/model.ckpt.index`). In
    this case, `from_tf` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the TensorFlow checkpoint in
    a PyTorch model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the PyTorch model afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **state_dict** (_Dict[str, torch.Tensor]_, _optional_) --
  A state dictionary to use instead of a state dictionary loaded from saved weights file.

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own
  weights. In this case though, you should check if using
  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the

    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForSpeechSeq2Seq

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForSpeechSeq2Seq.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForSpeechSeq2Seq.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)

```


## AutoModelForObjectDetection

<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained

  This option can be used if you want to create a model from a pretrained configuration but load your own

  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and

- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the

- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of

  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.

## AutoModelForImageSegmentation

<a id='transformers.AutoModelForImageSegmentation'></a>
> **class transformers.AutoModelForImageSegmentation**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a image segmentation head) when created

  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).

  [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and
  [from_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.from_pretrained) is not a simpler option.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_tf** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a TensorFlow checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, AutoModelForImageSegmentation

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = AutoModelForImageSegmentation.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = AutoModelForImageSegmentation.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a TF checkpoint file instead of a PyTorch model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_model_config.json')
>>> model = AutoModelForImageSegmentation.from_pretrained('./tf_model/bert_tf_checkpoint.ckpt.index', from_tf=True, config=config)
```


## TFAutoModel

<a id='transformers.TFAutoModel'></a>
> **class transformers.TFAutoModel**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the base model classes of the library when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the base model classes of the library from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [TFAlbertModel](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertModel) (ALBERT model)
  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [TFBartModel](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.TFBartModel) (BART model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [TFBertModel](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertModel) (BERT model)
  - [BlenderbotConfig](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.BlenderbotConfig) configuration class: [TFBlenderbotModel](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.TFBlenderbotModel) (Blenderbot model)
  - [BlenderbotSmallConfig](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.BlenderbotSmallConfig) configuration class: [TFBlenderbotSmallModel](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.TFBlenderbotSmallModel) (BlenderbotSmall model)
  - [CTRLConfig](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLConfig) configuration class: [TFCTRLModel](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.TFCTRLModel) (CTRL model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [TFCamembertModel](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertModel) (CamemBERT model)
  - [ConvBertConfig](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertConfig) configuration class: [TFConvBertModel](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.TFConvBertModel) (ConvBERT model)
  - [DPRConfig](model_doc/dpr.html#transformers.DPRConfig) configuration class: [TFDPRQuestionEncoder](model_doc/dpr.html#transformers.TFDPRQuestionEncoder) (DPR model)
  - [DebertaConfig](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaConfig) configuration class: [TFDebertaModel](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.TFDebertaModel) (DeBERTa model)
  - [DebertaV2Config](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Config) configuration class: [TFDebertaV2Model](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.TFDebertaV2Model) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [TFDistilBertModel](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertModel) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [TFElectraModel](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraModel) (ELECTRA model)
  - [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) configuration class: [TFFlaubertModel](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.TFFlaubertModel) (FlauBERT model)
  - [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) configuration class: [TFFunnelModel](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelModel) or [TFFunnelBaseModel](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelBaseModel) (Funnel Transformer model)
  - [GPT2Config](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Config) configuration class: [TFGPT2Model](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.TFGPT2Model) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
  - [HubertConfig](model_doc/hubert.html#transformers.HubertConfig) configuration class: [TFHubertModel](model_doc/hubert.html#transformers.TFHubertModel) (Hubert model)
  - [LEDConfig](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDConfig) configuration class: [TFLEDModel](model_doc/led.html#transformers.TFLEDModel) (LED model)
  - [LayoutLMConfig](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMConfig) configuration class: [TFLayoutLMModel](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.TFLayoutLMModel) (LayoutLM model)
  - [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) configuration class: [TFLongformerModel](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.TFLongformerModel) (Longformer model)
  - [LxmertConfig](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertConfig) configuration class: [TFLxmertModel](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.TFLxmertModel) (LXMERT model)
  - [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) configuration class: [TFMBartModel](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.TFMBartModel) (mBART model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [TFMPNetModel](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetModel) (MPNet model)
  - [MT5Config](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.MT5Config) configuration class: [TFMT5Model](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.TFMT5Model) (mT5 model)
  - [MarianConfig](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianConfig) configuration class: [TFMarianModel](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.TFMarianModel) (Marian model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [TFMobileBertModel](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertModel) (MobileBERT model)
  - [OpenAIGPTConfig](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTConfig) configuration class: [TFOpenAIGPTModel](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.TFOpenAIGPTModel) (OpenAI GPT model)
  - [PegasusConfig](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusConfig) configuration class: [TFPegasusModel](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.TFPegasusModel) (Pegasus model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [TFRemBertModel](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertModel) (RemBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [TFRoFormerModel](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerModel) (RoFormer model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFRobertaModel](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaModel) (RoBERTa model)
  - [T5Config](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Config) configuration class: [TFT5Model](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.TFT5Model) (T5 model)
  - [TransfoXLConfig](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLConfig) configuration class: [TFTransfoXLModel](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TFTransfoXLModel) (Transformer-XL model)
  - [Wav2Vec2Config](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2Config) configuration class: [TFWav2Vec2Model](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.TFWav2Vec2Model) (Wav2Vec2 model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMModel) (XLM model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMRobertaModel](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaModel) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [TFXLNetModel](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetModel) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModel
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = TFAutoModel.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the base model classes of the library from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [TFAlbertModel](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertModel) (ALBERT model)
- **bart** -- [TFBartModel](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.TFBartModel) (BART model)
- **bert** -- [TFBertModel](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertModel) (BERT model)
- **blenderbot** -- [TFBlenderbotModel](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.TFBlenderbotModel) (Blenderbot model)
- **blenderbot-small** -- [TFBlenderbotSmallModel](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.TFBlenderbotSmallModel) (BlenderbotSmall model)
- **camembert** -- [TFCamembertModel](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertModel) (CamemBERT model)
- **convbert** -- [TFConvBertModel](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.TFConvBertModel) (ConvBERT model)
- **ctrl** -- [TFCTRLModel](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.TFCTRLModel) (CTRL model)
- **deberta** -- [TFDebertaModel](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.TFDebertaModel) (DeBERTa model)
- **deberta-v2** -- [TFDebertaV2Model](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.TFDebertaV2Model) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
- **distilbert** -- [TFDistilBertModel](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertModel) (DistilBERT model)
- **dpr** -- [TFDPRQuestionEncoder](model_doc/dpr.html#transformers.TFDPRQuestionEncoder) (DPR model)
- **electra** -- [TFElectraModel](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraModel) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [TFFlaubertModel](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.TFFlaubertModel) (FlauBERT model)
- **funnel** -- [TFFunnelModel](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelModel) or [TFFunnelBaseModel](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelBaseModel) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **gpt2** -- [TFGPT2Model](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.TFGPT2Model) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
- **hubert** -- [TFHubertModel](model_doc/hubert.html#transformers.TFHubertModel) (Hubert model)
- **layoutlm** -- [TFLayoutLMModel](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.TFLayoutLMModel) (LayoutLM model)
- **led** -- [TFLEDModel](model_doc/led.html#transformers.TFLEDModel) (LED model)
- **longformer** -- [TFLongformerModel](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.TFLongformerModel) (Longformer model)
- **lxmert** -- [TFLxmertModel](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.TFLxmertModel) (LXMERT model)
- **marian** -- [TFMarianModel](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.TFMarianModel) (Marian model)
- **mbart** -- [TFMBartModel](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.TFMBartModel) (mBART model)
- **mobilebert** -- [TFMobileBertModel](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertModel) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [TFMPNetModel](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetModel) (MPNet model)
- **mt5** -- [TFMT5Model](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.TFMT5Model) (mT5 model)
- **openai-gpt** -- [TFOpenAIGPTModel](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.TFOpenAIGPTModel) (OpenAI GPT model)
- **pegasus** -- [TFPegasusModel](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.TFPegasusModel) (Pegasus model)
- **rembert** -- [TFRemBertModel](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertModel) (RemBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [TFRobertaModel](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaModel) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [TFRoFormerModel](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerModel) (RoFormer model)
- **t5** -- [TFT5Model](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.TFT5Model) (T5 model)
- **transfo-xl** -- [TFTransfoXLModel](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TFTransfoXLModel) (Transformer-XL model)
- **wav2vec2** -- [TFWav2Vec2Model](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.TFWav2Vec2Model) (Wav2Vec2 model)
- **xlm** -- [TFXLMModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMModel) (XLM model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [TFXLMRobertaModel](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaModel) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [TFXLNetModel](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetModel) (XLNet model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _PyTorch state_dict save file_ (e.g, `./pt_model/pytorch_model.bin`). In
    this case, `from_pt` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the PyTorch model in a
    TensorFlow model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the TensorFlow model
    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModel

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = TFAutoModel.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = TFAutoModel.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pt_model_config.json')
>>> model = TFAutoModel.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pytorch_model.bin', from_pt=True, config=config)
```


## TFAutoModelForPreTraining

<a id='transformers.TFAutoModelForPreTraining'></a>
> **class transformers.TFAutoModelForPreTraining**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a pretraining head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a pretraining head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [TFAlbertForPreTraining](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertForPreTraining) (ALBERT model)
  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [TFBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.TFBartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [TFBertForPreTraining](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertForPreTraining) (BERT model)
  - [CTRLConfig](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLConfig) configuration class: [TFCTRLLMHeadModel](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.TFCTRLLMHeadModel) (CTRL model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [TFCamembertForMaskedLM](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertForMaskedLM) (CamemBERT model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [TFDistilBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertForMaskedLM) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [TFElectraForPreTraining](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraForPreTraining) (ELECTRA model)
  - [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) configuration class: [TFFlaubertWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.TFFlaubertWithLMHeadModel) (FlauBERT model)
  - [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) configuration class: [TFFunnelForPreTraining](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelForPreTraining) (Funnel Transformer model)
  - [GPT2Config](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Config) configuration class: [TFGPT2LMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.TFGPT2LMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
  - [LayoutLMConfig](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMConfig) configuration class: [TFLayoutLMForMaskedLM](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.TFLayoutLMForMaskedLM) (LayoutLM model)
  - [LxmertConfig](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.LxmertConfig) configuration class: [TFLxmertForPreTraining](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.TFLxmertForPreTraining) (LXMERT model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [TFMPNetForMaskedLM](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetForMaskedLM) (MPNet model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [TFMobileBertForPreTraining](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertForPreTraining) (MobileBERT model)
  - [OpenAIGPTConfig](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTConfig) configuration class: [TFOpenAIGPTLMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.TFOpenAIGPTLMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaForMaskedLM) (RoBERTa model)
  - [T5Config](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Config) configuration class: [TFT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.TFT5ForConditionalGeneration) (T5 model)
  - [TransfoXLConfig](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLConfig) configuration class: [TFTransfoXLLMHeadModel](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TFTransfoXLLMHeadModel) (Transformer-XL model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMWithLMHeadModel) (XLM model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaForMaskedLM) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [TFXLNetLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetLMHeadModel) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForPreTraining
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForPreTraining.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a pretraining head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [TFAlbertForPreTraining](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertForPreTraining) (ALBERT model)
- **bart** -- [TFBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.TFBartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
- **bert** -- [TFBertForPreTraining](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertForPreTraining) (BERT model)
- **camembert** -- [TFCamembertForMaskedLM](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertForMaskedLM) (CamemBERT model)
- **ctrl** -- [TFCTRLLMHeadModel](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.TFCTRLLMHeadModel) (CTRL model)
- **distilbert** -- [TFDistilBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertForMaskedLM) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [TFElectraForPreTraining](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraForPreTraining) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [TFFlaubertWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.TFFlaubertWithLMHeadModel) (FlauBERT model)
- **funnel** -- [TFFunnelForPreTraining](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelForPreTraining) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **gpt2** -- [TFGPT2LMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.TFGPT2LMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
- **layoutlm** -- [TFLayoutLMForMaskedLM](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.TFLayoutLMForMaskedLM) (LayoutLM model)
- **lxmert** -- [TFLxmertForPreTraining](model_doc/lxmert.html#transformers.TFLxmertForPreTraining) (LXMERT model)
- **mobilebert** -- [TFMobileBertForPreTraining](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertForPreTraining) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [TFMPNetForMaskedLM](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetForMaskedLM) (MPNet model)
- **openai-gpt** -- [TFOpenAIGPTLMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.TFOpenAIGPTLMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT model)
- **roberta** -- [TFRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaForMaskedLM) (RoBERTa model)
- **t5** -- [TFT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.TFT5ForConditionalGeneration) (T5 model)
- **transfo-xl** -- [TFTransfoXLLMHeadModel](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TFTransfoXLLMHeadModel) (Transformer-XL model)
- **xlm** -- [TFXLMWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMWithLMHeadModel) (XLM model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [TFXLMRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaForMaskedLM) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [TFXLNetLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetLMHeadModel) (XLNet model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _PyTorch state_dict save file_ (e.g, `./pt_model/pytorch_model.bin`). In
    this case, `from_pt` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the PyTorch model in a
    TensorFlow model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the TensorFlow model
    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForPreTraining

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = TFAutoModelForPreTraining.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = TFAutoModelForPreTraining.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pt_model_config.json')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForPreTraining.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pytorch_model.bin', from_pt=True, config=config)
```


## TFAutoModelForCausalLM

<a id='transformers.TFAutoModelForCausalLM'></a>
> **class transformers.TFAutoModelForCausalLM**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a causal language modeling head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a causal language modeling head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [TFBertLMHeadModel](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertLMHeadModel) (BERT model)
  - [CTRLConfig](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLConfig) configuration class: [TFCTRLLMHeadModel](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.TFCTRLLMHeadModel) (CTRL model)
  - [GPT2Config](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Config) configuration class: [TFGPT2LMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.TFGPT2LMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
  - [OpenAIGPTConfig](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTConfig) configuration class: [TFOpenAIGPTLMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.TFOpenAIGPTLMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [TFRemBertForCausalLM](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertForCausalLM) (RemBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [TFRoFormerForCausalLM](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerForCausalLM) (RoFormer model)
  - [TransfoXLConfig](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLConfig) configuration class: [TFTransfoXLLMHeadModel](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TFTransfoXLLMHeadModel) (Transformer-XL model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMWithLMHeadModel) (XLM model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [TFXLNetLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetLMHeadModel) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForCausalLM
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForCausalLM.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a causal language modeling head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **bert** -- [TFBertLMHeadModel](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertLMHeadModel) (BERT model)
- **ctrl** -- [TFCTRLLMHeadModel](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.TFCTRLLMHeadModel) (CTRL model)
- **gpt2** -- [TFGPT2LMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.TFGPT2LMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
- **openai-gpt** -- [TFOpenAIGPTLMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.TFOpenAIGPTLMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT model)
- **rembert** -- [TFRemBertForCausalLM](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertForCausalLM) (RemBERT model)
- **roformer** -- [TFRoFormerForCausalLM](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerForCausalLM) (RoFormer model)
- **transfo-xl** -- [TFTransfoXLLMHeadModel](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TFTransfoXLLMHeadModel) (Transformer-XL model)
- **xlm** -- [TFXLMWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMWithLMHeadModel) (XLM model)
- **xlnet** -- [TFXLNetLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetLMHeadModel) (XLNet model)

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _PyTorch state_dict save file_ (e.g, `./pt_model/pytorch_model.bin`). In

    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the PyTorch model in a
    TensorFlow model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the TensorFlow model
    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForCausalLM

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = TFAutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = TFAutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
```
