

## TFAutoModelForMaskedLM

<a id='transformers.TFAutoModelForMaskedLM'></a>
> **class transformers.TFAutoModelForMaskedLM**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a masked language modeling head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a masked language modeling head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [TFAlbertForMaskedLM](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertForMaskedLM) (ALBERT model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [TFBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertForMaskedLM) (BERT model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [TFCamembertForMaskedLM](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertForMaskedLM) (CamemBERT model)
  - [ConvBertConfig](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertConfig) configuration class: [TFConvBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.TFConvBertForMaskedLM) (ConvBERT model)
  - [DebertaConfig](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaConfig) configuration class: [TFDebertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.TFDebertaForMaskedLM) (DeBERTa model)
  - [DebertaV2Config](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Config) configuration class: [TFDebertaV2ForMaskedLM](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.TFDebertaV2ForMaskedLM) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [TFDistilBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertForMaskedLM) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [TFElectraForMaskedLM](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraForMaskedLM) (ELECTRA model)
  - [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) configuration class: [TFFlaubertWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.TFFlaubertWithLMHeadModel) (FlauBERT model)
  - [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) configuration class: [TFFunnelForMaskedLM](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelForMaskedLM) (Funnel Transformer model)
  - [LayoutLMConfig](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMConfig) configuration class: [TFLayoutLMForMaskedLM](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.TFLayoutLMForMaskedLM) (LayoutLM model)
  - [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) configuration class: [TFLongformerForMaskedLM](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.TFLongformerForMaskedLM) (Longformer model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [TFMPNetForMaskedLM](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetForMaskedLM) (MPNet model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [TFMobileBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertForMaskedLM) (MobileBERT model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [TFRemBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertForMaskedLM) (RemBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [TFRoFormerForMaskedLM](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerForMaskedLM) (RoFormer model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaForMaskedLM) (RoBERTa model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMWithLMHeadModel) (XLM model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaForMaskedLM) (XLM-RoBERTa model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForMaskedLM
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForMaskedLM.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a masked language modeling head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [TFAlbertForMaskedLM](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertForMaskedLM) (ALBERT model)
- **bert** -- [TFBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertForMaskedLM) (BERT model)
- **camembert** -- [TFCamembertForMaskedLM](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertForMaskedLM) (CamemBERT model)
- **convbert** -- [TFConvBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.TFConvBertForMaskedLM) (ConvBERT model)
- **deberta** -- [TFDebertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.TFDebertaForMaskedLM) (DeBERTa model)
- **deberta-v2** -- [TFDebertaV2ForMaskedLM](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.TFDebertaV2ForMaskedLM) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
- **distilbert** -- [TFDistilBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertForMaskedLM) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [TFElectraForMaskedLM](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraForMaskedLM) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [TFFlaubertWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.TFFlaubertWithLMHeadModel) (FlauBERT model)
- **funnel** -- [TFFunnelForMaskedLM](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelForMaskedLM) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **layoutlm** -- [TFLayoutLMForMaskedLM](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.TFLayoutLMForMaskedLM) (LayoutLM model)
- **longformer** -- [TFLongformerForMaskedLM](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.TFLongformerForMaskedLM) (Longformer model)
- **mobilebert** -- [TFMobileBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertForMaskedLM) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [TFMPNetForMaskedLM](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetForMaskedLM) (MPNet model)
- **rembert** -- [TFRemBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertForMaskedLM) (RemBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [TFRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaForMaskedLM) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [TFRoFormerForMaskedLM](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerForMaskedLM) (RoFormer model)
- **xlm** -- [TFXLMWithLMHeadModel](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMWithLMHeadModel) (XLM model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [TFXLMRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaForMaskedLM) (XLM-RoBERTa model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _PyTorch state_dict save file_ (e.g, `./pt_model/pytorch_model.bin`). In
    this case, `from_pt` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the PyTorch model in a
    TensorFlow model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the TensorFlow model
    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForMaskedLM

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = TFAutoModelForMaskedLM.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = TFAutoModelForMaskedLM.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pt_model_config.json')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForMaskedLM.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pytorch_model.bin', from_pt=True, config=config)
```


## TFAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM

<a id='transformers.TFAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM'></a>
> **class transformers.TFAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence-to-sequence language modeling head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence-to-sequence language modeling head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [TFBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.TFBartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
  - [BlenderbotConfig](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.BlenderbotConfig) configuration class: [TFBlenderbotForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.TFBlenderbotForConditionalGeneration) (Blenderbot model)
  - [BlenderbotSmallConfig](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.BlenderbotSmallConfig) configuration class: [TFBlenderbotSmallForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.TFBlenderbotSmallForConditionalGeneration) (BlenderbotSmall model)
  - [LEDConfig](model_doc/led.html#transformers.LEDConfig) configuration class: [TFLEDForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/led.html#transformers.TFLEDForConditionalGeneration) (LED model)
  - [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) configuration class: [TFMBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.TFMBartForConditionalGeneration) (mBART model)
  - [MT5Config](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.MT5Config) configuration class: [TFMT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.TFMT5ForConditionalGeneration) (mT5 model)
  - [MarianConfig](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianConfig) configuration class: [TFMarianMTModel](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.TFMarianMTModel) (Marian model)
  - [PegasusConfig](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusConfig) configuration class: [TFPegasusForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.TFPegasusForConditionalGeneration) (Pegasus model)
  - [T5Config](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Config) configuration class: [TFT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.TFT5ForConditionalGeneration) (T5 model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('t5-base')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence-to-sequence language modeling head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **bart** -- [TFBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.TFBartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
- **blenderbot** -- [TFBlenderbotForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/blenderbot.html#transformers.TFBlenderbotForConditionalGeneration) (Blenderbot model)
- **blenderbot-small** -- [TFBlenderbotSmallForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/blenderbot_small.html#transformers.TFBlenderbotSmallForConditionalGeneration) (BlenderbotSmall model)
- **led** -- [TFLEDForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/led.html#transformers.TFLEDForConditionalGeneration) (LED model)
- **marian** -- [TFMarianMTModel](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.TFMarianMTModel) (Marian model)
- **mbart** -- [TFMBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.TFMBartForConditionalGeneration) (mBART model)
- **mt5** -- [TFMT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.TFMT5ForConditionalGeneration) (mT5 model)
- **pegasus** -- [TFPegasusForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.TFPegasusForConditionalGeneration) (Pegasus model)
- **t5** -- [TFT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.TFT5ForConditionalGeneration) (T5 model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _PyTorch state_dict save file_ (e.g, `./pt_model/pytorch_model.bin`). In
    this case, `from_pt` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the PyTorch model in a
    TensorFlow model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the TensorFlow model
    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = TFAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM.from_pretrained('t5-base')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = TFAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM.from_pretrained('t5-base', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./pt_model/t5_pt_model_config.json')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM.from_pretrained('./pt_model/t5_pytorch_model.bin', from_pt=True, config=config)
```


## TFAutoModelForSequenceClassification

<a id='transformers.TFAutoModelForSequenceClassification'></a>
> **class transformers.TFAutoModelForSequenceClassification**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence classification head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence classification head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [TFAlbertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertForSequenceClassification) (ALBERT model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [TFBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertForSequenceClassification) (BERT model)
  - [CTRLConfig](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.CTRLConfig) configuration class: [TFCTRLForSequenceClassification](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.TFCTRLForSequenceClassification) (CTRL model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [TFCamembertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertForSequenceClassification) (CamemBERT model)
  - [ConvBertConfig](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertConfig) configuration class: [TFConvBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.TFConvBertForSequenceClassification) (ConvBERT model)
  - [DebertaConfig](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaConfig) configuration class: [TFDebertaForSequenceClassification](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.TFDebertaForSequenceClassification) (DeBERTa model)
  - [DebertaV2Config](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Config) configuration class: [TFDebertaV2ForSequenceClassification](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.TFDebertaV2ForSequenceClassification) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [TFDistilBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertForSequenceClassification) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [TFElectraForSequenceClassification](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraForSequenceClassification) (ELECTRA model)
  - [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) configuration class: [TFFlaubertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.TFFlaubertForSequenceClassification) (FlauBERT model)
  - [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) configuration class: [TFFunnelForSequenceClassification](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelForSequenceClassification) (Funnel Transformer model)
  - [GPT2Config](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Config) configuration class: [TFGPT2ForSequenceClassification](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.TFGPT2ForSequenceClassification) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
  - [LayoutLMConfig](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMConfig) configuration class: [TFLayoutLMForSequenceClassification](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.TFLayoutLMForSequenceClassification) (LayoutLM model)
  - [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) configuration class: [TFLongformerForSequenceClassification](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.TFLongformerForSequenceClassification) (Longformer model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [TFMPNetForSequenceClassification](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetForSequenceClassification) (MPNet model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [TFMobileBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertForSequenceClassification) (MobileBERT model)
  - [OpenAIGPTConfig](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.OpenAIGPTConfig) configuration class: [TFOpenAIGPTForSequenceClassification](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.TFOpenAIGPTForSequenceClassification) (OpenAI GPT model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [TFRemBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertForSequenceClassification) (RemBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [TFRoFormerForSequenceClassification](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerForSequenceClassification) (RoFormer model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFRobertaForSequenceClassification](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaForSequenceClassification) (RoBERTa model)
  - [TransfoXLConfig](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TransfoXLConfig) configuration class: [TFTransfoXLForSequenceClassification](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TFTransfoXLForSequenceClassification) (Transformer-XL model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMForSequenceClassification](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMForSequenceClassification) (XLM model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMRobertaForSequenceClassification](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaForSequenceClassification) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [TFXLNetForSequenceClassification](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetForSequenceClassification) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForSequenceClassification
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence classification head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [TFAlbertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertForSequenceClassification) (ALBERT model)
- **bert** -- [TFBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertForSequenceClassification) (BERT model)
- **camembert** -- [TFCamembertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertForSequenceClassification) (CamemBERT model)
- **convbert** -- [TFConvBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.TFConvBertForSequenceClassification) (ConvBERT model)
- **ctrl** -- [TFCTRLForSequenceClassification](model_doc/ctrl.html#transformers.TFCTRLForSequenceClassification) (CTRL model)
- **deberta** -- [TFDebertaForSequenceClassification](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.TFDebertaForSequenceClassification) (DeBERTa model)
- **deberta-v2** -- [TFDebertaV2ForSequenceClassification](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.TFDebertaV2ForSequenceClassification) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
- **distilbert** -- [TFDistilBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertForSequenceClassification) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [TFElectraForSequenceClassification](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraForSequenceClassification) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [TFFlaubertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.TFFlaubertForSequenceClassification) (FlauBERT model)
- **funnel** -- [TFFunnelForSequenceClassification](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelForSequenceClassification) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **gpt2** -- [TFGPT2ForSequenceClassification](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.TFGPT2ForSequenceClassification) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
- **layoutlm** -- [TFLayoutLMForSequenceClassification](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.TFLayoutLMForSequenceClassification) (LayoutLM model)
- **longformer** -- [TFLongformerForSequenceClassification](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.TFLongformerForSequenceClassification) (Longformer model)
- **mobilebert** -- [TFMobileBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertForSequenceClassification) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [TFMPNetForSequenceClassification](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetForSequenceClassification) (MPNet model)
- **openai-gpt** -- [TFOpenAIGPTForSequenceClassification](model_doc/gpt.html#transformers.TFOpenAIGPTForSequenceClassification) (OpenAI GPT model)
- **rembert** -- [TFRemBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertForSequenceClassification) (RemBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [TFRobertaForSequenceClassification](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaForSequenceClassification) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [TFRoFormerForSequenceClassification](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerForSequenceClassification) (RoFormer model)
- **transfo-xl** -- [TFTransfoXLForSequenceClassification](model_doc/transformerxl.html#transformers.TFTransfoXLForSequenceClassification) (Transformer-XL model)
- **xlm** -- [TFXLMForSequenceClassification](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMForSequenceClassification) (XLM model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [TFXLMRobertaForSequenceClassification](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaForSequenceClassification) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [TFXLNetForSequenceClassification](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetForSequenceClassification) (XLNet model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _PyTorch state_dict save file_ (e.g, `./pt_model/pytorch_model.bin`). In
    this case, `from_pt` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the PyTorch model in a
    TensorFlow model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the TensorFlow model
    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForSequenceClassification

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = TFAutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = TFAutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pt_model_config.json')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pytorch_model.bin', from_pt=True, config=config)
```


## TFAutoModelForMultipleChoice

<a id='transformers.TFAutoModelForMultipleChoice'></a>
> **class transformers.TFAutoModelForMultipleChoice**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a multiple choice head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a multiple choice head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [TFAlbertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertForMultipleChoice) (ALBERT model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [TFBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertForMultipleChoice) (BERT model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [TFCamembertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertForMultipleChoice) (CamemBERT model)
  - [ConvBertConfig](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertConfig) configuration class: [TFConvBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.TFConvBertForMultipleChoice) (ConvBERT model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [TFDistilBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertForMultipleChoice) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [TFElectraForMultipleChoice](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraForMultipleChoice) (ELECTRA model)
  - [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) configuration class: [TFFlaubertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.TFFlaubertForMultipleChoice) (FlauBERT model)
  - [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) configuration class: [TFFunnelForMultipleChoice](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelForMultipleChoice) (Funnel Transformer model)
  - [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) configuration class: [TFLongformerForMultipleChoice](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.TFLongformerForMultipleChoice) (Longformer model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [TFMPNetForMultipleChoice](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetForMultipleChoice) (MPNet model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [TFMobileBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertForMultipleChoice) (MobileBERT model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [TFRemBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertForMultipleChoice) (RemBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [TFRoFormerForMultipleChoice](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerForMultipleChoice) (RoFormer model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFRobertaForMultipleChoice](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaForMultipleChoice) (RoBERTa model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMForMultipleChoice](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMForMultipleChoice) (XLM model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMRobertaForMultipleChoice](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaForMultipleChoice) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [TFXLNetForMultipleChoice](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetForMultipleChoice) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForMultipleChoice
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForMultipleChoice.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a multiple choice head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [TFAlbertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertForMultipleChoice) (ALBERT model)
- **bert** -- [TFBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertForMultipleChoice) (BERT model)
- **camembert** -- [TFCamembertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertForMultipleChoice) (CamemBERT model)
- **convbert** -- [TFConvBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.TFConvBertForMultipleChoice) (ConvBERT model)
- **distilbert** -- [TFDistilBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertForMultipleChoice) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [TFElectraForMultipleChoice](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraForMultipleChoice) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [TFFlaubertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.TFFlaubertForMultipleChoice) (FlauBERT model)
- **funnel** -- [TFFunnelForMultipleChoice](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelForMultipleChoice) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **longformer** -- [TFLongformerForMultipleChoice](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.TFLongformerForMultipleChoice) (Longformer model)
- **mobilebert** -- [TFMobileBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertForMultipleChoice) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [TFMPNetForMultipleChoice](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetForMultipleChoice) (MPNet model)
- **rembert** -- [TFRemBertForMultipleChoice](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertForMultipleChoice) (RemBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [TFRobertaForMultipleChoice](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaForMultipleChoice) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [TFRoFormerForMultipleChoice](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerForMultipleChoice) (RoFormer model)
- **xlm** -- [TFXLMForMultipleChoice](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMForMultipleChoice) (XLM model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [TFXLMRobertaForMultipleChoice](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaForMultipleChoice) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [TFXLNetForMultipleChoice](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetForMultipleChoice) (XLNet model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _PyTorch state_dict save file_ (e.g, `./pt_model/pytorch_model.bin`). In
    this case, `from_pt` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the PyTorch model in a
    TensorFlow model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the TensorFlow model
    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForMultipleChoice

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = TFAutoModelForMultipleChoice.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = TFAutoModelForMultipleChoice.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pt_model_config.json')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForMultipleChoice.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pytorch_model.bin', from_pt=True, config=config)
```


## TFAutoModelForTokenClassification

<a id='transformers.TFAutoModelForTokenClassification'></a>
> **class transformers.TFAutoModelForTokenClassification**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a token classification head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a token classification head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [TFAlbertForTokenClassification](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertForTokenClassification) (ALBERT model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [TFBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertForTokenClassification) (BERT model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [TFCamembertForTokenClassification](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertForTokenClassification) (CamemBERT model)
  - [ConvBertConfig](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertConfig) configuration class: [TFConvBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.TFConvBertForTokenClassification) (ConvBERT model)
  - [DebertaConfig](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaConfig) configuration class: [TFDebertaForTokenClassification](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.TFDebertaForTokenClassification) (DeBERTa model)
  - [DebertaV2Config](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Config) configuration class: [TFDebertaV2ForTokenClassification](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.TFDebertaV2ForTokenClassification) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [TFDistilBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertForTokenClassification) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [TFElectraForTokenClassification](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraForTokenClassification) (ELECTRA model)
