  - [LayoutLMConfig](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.LayoutLMConfig) configuration class: [TFLayoutLMForTokenClassification](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.TFLayoutLMForTokenClassification) (LayoutLM model)
  - [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) configuration class: [TFLongformerForTokenClassification](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.TFLongformerForTokenClassification) (Longformer model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [TFMPNetForTokenClassification](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetForTokenClassification) (MPNet model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [TFMobileBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertForTokenClassification) (MobileBERT model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [TFRemBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertForTokenClassification) (RemBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [TFRoFormerForTokenClassification](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerForTokenClassification) (RoFormer model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFRobertaForTokenClassification](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaForTokenClassification) (RoBERTa model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMForTokenClassification](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMForTokenClassification) (XLM model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMRobertaForTokenClassification](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaForTokenClassification) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [TFXLNetForTokenClassification](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetForTokenClassification) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForTokenClassification
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForTokenClassification.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a token classification head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [TFAlbertForTokenClassification](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertForTokenClassification) (ALBERT model)
- **bert** -- [TFBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertForTokenClassification) (BERT model)
- **camembert** -- [TFCamembertForTokenClassification](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertForTokenClassification) (CamemBERT model)
- **convbert** -- [TFConvBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.TFConvBertForTokenClassification) (ConvBERT model)
- **deberta** -- [TFDebertaForTokenClassification](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.TFDebertaForTokenClassification) (DeBERTa model)
- **deberta-v2** -- [TFDebertaV2ForTokenClassification](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.TFDebertaV2ForTokenClassification) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
- **distilbert** -- [TFDistilBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertForTokenClassification) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [TFElectraForTokenClassification](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraForTokenClassification) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [TFFlaubertForTokenClassification](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.TFFlaubertForTokenClassification) (FlauBERT model)
- **funnel** -- [TFFunnelForTokenClassification](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelForTokenClassification) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **layoutlm** -- [TFLayoutLMForTokenClassification](model_doc/layoutlm.html#transformers.TFLayoutLMForTokenClassification) (LayoutLM model)
- **longformer** -- [TFLongformerForTokenClassification](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.TFLongformerForTokenClassification) (Longformer model)
- **mobilebert** -- [TFMobileBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertForTokenClassification) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [TFMPNetForTokenClassification](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetForTokenClassification) (MPNet model)
- **rembert** -- [TFRemBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertForTokenClassification) (RemBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [TFRobertaForTokenClassification](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaForTokenClassification) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [TFRoFormerForTokenClassification](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerForTokenClassification) (RoFormer model)
- **xlm** -- [TFXLMForTokenClassification](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMForTokenClassification) (XLM model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [TFXLMRobertaForTokenClassification](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaForTokenClassification) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [TFXLNetForTokenClassification](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetForTokenClassification) (XLNet model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _PyTorch state_dict save file_ (e.g, `./pt_model/pytorch_model.bin`). In
    this case, `from_pt` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the PyTorch model in a
    TensorFlow model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the TensorFlow model
    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForTokenClassification

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = TFAutoModelForTokenClassification.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = TFAutoModelForTokenClassification.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pt_model_config.json')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForTokenClassification.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pytorch_model.bin', from_pt=True, config=config)
```


## TFAutoModelForQuestionAnswering

<a id='transformers.TFAutoModelForQuestionAnswering'></a>
> **class transformers.TFAutoModelForQuestionAnswering**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a question answering head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a question answering head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [TFAlbertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertForQuestionAnswering) (ALBERT model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [TFBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertForQuestionAnswering) (BERT model)
  - [CamembertConfig](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.CamembertConfig) configuration class: [TFCamembertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertForQuestionAnswering) (CamemBERT model)
  - [ConvBertConfig](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.ConvBertConfig) configuration class: [TFConvBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.TFConvBertForQuestionAnswering) (ConvBERT model)
  - [DebertaConfig](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.DebertaConfig) configuration class: [TFDebertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.TFDebertaForQuestionAnswering) (DeBERTa model)
  - [DebertaV2Config](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.DebertaV2Config) configuration class: [TFDebertaV2ForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.TFDebertaV2ForQuestionAnswering) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [TFDistilBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertForQuestionAnswering) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [TFElectraForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraForQuestionAnswering) (ELECTRA model)
  - [FlaubertConfig](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.FlaubertConfig) configuration class: [TFFlaubertForQuestionAnsweringSimple](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.TFFlaubertForQuestionAnsweringSimple) (FlauBERT model)
  - [FunnelConfig](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.FunnelConfig) configuration class: [TFFunnelForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelForQuestionAnswering) (Funnel Transformer model)
  - [LongformerConfig](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.LongformerConfig) configuration class: [TFLongformerForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.TFLongformerForQuestionAnswering) (Longformer model)
  - [MPNetConfig](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.MPNetConfig) configuration class: [TFMPNetForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetForQuestionAnswering) (MPNet model)
  - [MobileBertConfig](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.MobileBertConfig) configuration class: [TFMobileBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertForQuestionAnswering) (MobileBERT model)
  - [RemBertConfig](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.RemBertConfig) configuration class: [TFRemBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertForQuestionAnswering) (RemBERT model)
  - [RoFormerConfig](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.RoFormerConfig) configuration class: [TFRoFormerForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerForQuestionAnswering) (RoFormer model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFRobertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaForQuestionAnswering) (RoBERTa model)
  - [XLMConfig](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.XLMConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMForQuestionAnsweringSimple](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMForQuestionAnsweringSimple) (XLM model)
  - [XLMRobertaConfig](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.XLMRobertaConfig) configuration class: [TFXLMRobertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaForQuestionAnswering) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
  - [XLNetConfig](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.XLNetConfig) configuration class: [TFXLNetForQuestionAnsweringSimple](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetForQuestionAnsweringSimple) (XLNet model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForQuestionAnswering
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForQuestionAnswering.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a question answering head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [TFAlbertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.TFAlbertForQuestionAnswering) (ALBERT model)
- **bert** -- [TFBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.TFBertForQuestionAnswering) (BERT model)
- **camembert** -- [TFCamembertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/camembert.html#transformers.TFCamembertForQuestionAnswering) (CamemBERT model)
- **convbert** -- [TFConvBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/convbert.html#transformers.TFConvBertForQuestionAnswering) (ConvBERT model)
- **deberta** -- [TFDebertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/deberta.html#transformers.TFDebertaForQuestionAnswering) (DeBERTa model)
- **deberta-v2** -- [TFDebertaV2ForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/deberta_v2.html#transformers.TFDebertaV2ForQuestionAnswering) (DeBERTa-v2 model)
- **distilbert** -- [TFDistilBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.TFDistilBertForQuestionAnswering) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [TFElectraForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.TFElectraForQuestionAnswering) (ELECTRA model)
- **flaubert** -- [TFFlaubertForQuestionAnsweringSimple](model_doc/flaubert.html#transformers.TFFlaubertForQuestionAnsweringSimple) (FlauBERT model)
- **funnel** -- [TFFunnelForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/funnel.html#transformers.TFFunnelForQuestionAnswering) (Funnel Transformer model)
- **longformer** -- [TFLongformerForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/longformer.html#transformers.TFLongformerForQuestionAnswering) (Longformer model)
- **mobilebert** -- [TFMobileBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/mobilebert.html#transformers.TFMobileBertForQuestionAnswering) (MobileBERT model)
- **mpnet** -- [TFMPNetForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/mpnet.html#transformers.TFMPNetForQuestionAnswering) (MPNet model)
- **rembert** -- [TFRemBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/rembert.html#transformers.TFRemBertForQuestionAnswering) (RemBERT model)
- **roberta** -- [TFRobertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.TFRobertaForQuestionAnswering) (RoBERTa model)
- **roformer** -- [TFRoFormerForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/roformer.html#transformers.TFRoFormerForQuestionAnswering) (RoFormer model)
- **xlm** -- [TFXLMForQuestionAnsweringSimple](model_doc/xlm.html#transformers.TFXLMForQuestionAnsweringSimple) (XLM model)
- **xlm-roberta** -- [TFXLMRobertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/xlmroberta.html#transformers.TFXLMRobertaForQuestionAnswering) (XLM-RoBERTa model)
- **xlnet** -- [TFXLNetForQuestionAnsweringSimple](model_doc/xlnet.html#transformers.TFXLNetForQuestionAnsweringSimple) (XLNet model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _PyTorch state_dict save file_ (e.g, `./pt_model/pytorch_model.bin`). In
    this case, `from_pt` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the PyTorch model in a
    TensorFlow model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the TensorFlow model
    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, TFAutoModelForQuestionAnswering

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = TFAutoModelForQuestionAnswering.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = TFAutoModelForQuestionAnswering.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pt_model_config.json')
>>> model = TFAutoModelForQuestionAnswering.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pytorch_model.bin', from_pt=True, config=config)
```


## FlaxAutoModel

<a id='transformers.FlaxAutoModel'></a>
> **class transformers.FlaxAutoModel**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the base model classes of the library when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the base model classes of the library from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxAlbertModel](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.FlaxAlbertModel) (ALBERT model)
  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBartModel](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.FlaxBartModel) (BART model)
  - [BeitConfig](model_doc/beit.html#transformers.BeitConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBeitModel](model_doc/beit.html#transformers.FlaxBeitModel) (BeiT model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBertModel](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.FlaxBertModel) (BERT model)
  - [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBigBirdModel](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.FlaxBigBirdModel) (BigBird model)
  - [CLIPConfig](model_doc/clip.html#transformers.CLIPConfig) configuration class: [FlaxCLIPModel](model_doc/clip.html#transformers.FlaxCLIPModel) (CLIP model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxDistilBertModel](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.FlaxDistilBertModel) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [FlaxElectraModel](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.FlaxElectraModel) (ELECTRA model)
  - [GPT2Config](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Config) configuration class: [FlaxGPT2Model](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.FlaxGPT2Model) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
  - [GPTNeoConfig](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.GPTNeoConfig) configuration class: [FlaxGPTNeoModel](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.FlaxGPTNeoModel) (GPT Neo model)
  - [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) configuration class: [FlaxMBartModel](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.FlaxMBartModel) (mBART model)
  - [MT5Config](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.MT5Config) configuration class: [FlaxMT5Model](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.FlaxMT5Model) (mT5 model)
  - [MarianConfig](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianConfig) configuration class: [FlaxMarianModel](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.FlaxMarianModel) (Marian model)
  - [PegasusConfig](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusConfig) configuration class: [FlaxPegasusModel](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.FlaxPegasusModel) (Pegasus model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [FlaxRobertaModel](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.FlaxRobertaModel) (RoBERTa model)
  - [T5Config](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Config) configuration class: [FlaxT5Model](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.FlaxT5Model) (T5 model)
  - [ViTConfig](model_doc/vit.html#transformers.ViTConfig) configuration class: [FlaxViTModel](model_doc/vit.html#transformers.FlaxViTModel) (ViT model)
  - [Wav2Vec2Config](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2Config) configuration class: [FlaxWav2Vec2Model](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.FlaxWav2Vec2Model) (Wav2Vec2 model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, FlaxAutoModel
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = FlaxAutoModel.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the base model classes of the library from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [FlaxAlbertModel](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.FlaxAlbertModel) (ALBERT model)
- **bart** -- [FlaxBartModel](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.FlaxBartModel) (BART model)
- **beit** -- [FlaxBeitModel](model_doc/beit.html#transformers.FlaxBeitModel) (BeiT model)
- **bert** -- [FlaxBertModel](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.FlaxBertModel) (BERT model)
- **big_bird** -- [FlaxBigBirdModel](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.FlaxBigBirdModel) (BigBird model)
- **clip** -- [FlaxCLIPModel](model_doc/clip.html#transformers.FlaxCLIPModel) (CLIP model)
- **distilbert** -- [FlaxDistilBertModel](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.FlaxDistilBertModel) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [FlaxElectraModel](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.FlaxElectraModel) (ELECTRA model)
- **gpt2** -- [FlaxGPT2Model](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.FlaxGPT2Model) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
- **gpt_neo** -- [FlaxGPTNeoModel](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.FlaxGPTNeoModel) (GPT Neo model)
- **marian** -- [FlaxMarianModel](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.FlaxMarianModel) (Marian model)
- **mbart** -- [FlaxMBartModel](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.FlaxMBartModel) (mBART model)
- **mt5** -- [FlaxMT5Model](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.FlaxMT5Model) (mT5 model)
- **pegasus** -- [FlaxPegasusModel](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.FlaxPegasusModel) (Pegasus model)
- **roberta** -- [FlaxRobertaModel](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.FlaxRobertaModel) (RoBERTa model)
- **t5** -- [FlaxT5Model](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.FlaxT5Model) (T5 model)
- **vit** -- [FlaxViTModel](model_doc/vit.html#transformers.FlaxViTModel) (ViT model)
- **wav2vec2** -- [FlaxWav2Vec2Model](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.FlaxWav2Vec2Model) (Wav2Vec2 model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _PyTorch state_dict save file_ (e.g, `./pt_model/pytorch_model.bin`). In
    this case, `from_pt` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the PyTorch model in a
    TensorFlow model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the TensorFlow model
    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, FlaxAutoModel

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = FlaxAutoModel.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = FlaxAutoModel.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pt_model_config.json')
>>> model = FlaxAutoModel.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pytorch_model.bin', from_pt=True, config=config)
```


## FlaxAutoModelForCausalLM

<a id='transformers.FlaxAutoModelForCausalLM'></a>
> **class transformers.FlaxAutoModelForCausalLM**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a causal language modeling head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a causal language modeling head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [GPT2Config](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.GPT2Config) configuration class: [FlaxGPT2LMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.FlaxGPT2LMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
  - [GPTNeoConfig](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.GPTNeoConfig) configuration class: [FlaxGPTNeoForCausalLM](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.FlaxGPTNeoForCausalLM) (GPT Neo model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, FlaxAutoModelForCausalLM
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForCausalLM.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a causal language modeling head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **gpt2** -- [FlaxGPT2LMHeadModel](model_doc/gpt2.html#transformers.FlaxGPT2LMHeadModel) (OpenAI GPT-2 model)
- **gpt_neo** -- [FlaxGPTNeoForCausalLM](model_doc/gpt_neo.html#transformers.FlaxGPTNeoForCausalLM) (GPT Neo model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _PyTorch state_dict save file_ (e.g, `./pt_model/pytorch_model.bin`). In
    this case, `from_pt` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the PyTorch model in a
    TensorFlow model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the TensorFlow model
    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, FlaxAutoModelForCausalLM

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pt_model_config.json')
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pytorch_model.bin', from_pt=True, config=config)
```


## FlaxAutoModelForPreTraining

<a id='transformers.FlaxAutoModelForPreTraining'></a>
> **class transformers.FlaxAutoModelForPreTraining**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a pretraining head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a pretraining head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxAlbertForPreTraining](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.FlaxAlbertForPreTraining) (ALBERT model)
  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.FlaxBartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBertForPreTraining](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.FlaxBertForPreTraining) (BERT model)
  - [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBigBirdForPreTraining](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.FlaxBigBirdForPreTraining) (BigBird model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [FlaxElectraForPreTraining](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.FlaxElectraForPreTraining) (ELECTRA model)
  - [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) configuration class: [FlaxMBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.FlaxMBartForConditionalGeneration) (mBART model)
  - [MT5Config](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.MT5Config) configuration class: [FlaxMT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.FlaxMT5ForConditionalGeneration) (mT5 model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [FlaxRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.FlaxRobertaForMaskedLM) (RoBERTa model)
  - [T5Config](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Config) configuration class: [FlaxT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.FlaxT5ForConditionalGeneration) (T5 model)
  - [Wav2Vec2Config](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.Wav2Vec2Config) configuration class: [FlaxWav2Vec2ForPreTraining](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.FlaxWav2Vec2ForPreTraining) (Wav2Vec2 model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, FlaxAutoModelForPreTraining
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForPreTraining.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a pretraining head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [FlaxAlbertForPreTraining](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.FlaxAlbertForPreTraining) (ALBERT model)
- **bart** -- [FlaxBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.FlaxBartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
- **bert** -- [FlaxBertForPreTraining](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.FlaxBertForPreTraining) (BERT model)
- **big_bird** -- [FlaxBigBirdForPreTraining](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.FlaxBigBirdForPreTraining) (BigBird model)
- **electra** -- [FlaxElectraForPreTraining](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.FlaxElectraForPreTraining) (ELECTRA model)
- **mbart** -- [FlaxMBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.FlaxMBartForConditionalGeneration) (mBART model)
- **mt5** -- [FlaxMT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.FlaxMT5ForConditionalGeneration) (mT5 model)
- **roberta** -- [FlaxRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.FlaxRobertaForMaskedLM) (RoBERTa model)
- **t5** -- [FlaxT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.FlaxT5ForConditionalGeneration) (T5 model)
- **wav2vec2** -- [FlaxWav2Vec2ForPreTraining](model_doc/wav2vec2.html#transformers.FlaxWav2Vec2ForPreTraining) (Wav2Vec2 model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under

    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.

  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.

- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --

  automatically loaded:

    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, FlaxAutoModelForPreTraining
```

## FlaxAutoModelForMaskedLM

<a id='transformers.FlaxAutoModelForMaskedLM'></a>
> **class transformers.FlaxAutoModelForMaskedLM**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a masked language modeling head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a masked language modeling head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxAlbertForMaskedLM](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.FlaxAlbertForMaskedLM) (ALBERT model)
  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.FlaxBartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.FlaxBertForMaskedLM) (BERT model)
  - [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBigBirdForMaskedLM](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.FlaxBigBirdForMaskedLM) (BigBird model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxDistilBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.FlaxDistilBertForMaskedLM) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [FlaxElectraForMaskedLM](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.FlaxElectraForMaskedLM) (ELECTRA model)
  - [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) configuration class: [FlaxMBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.FlaxMBartForConditionalGeneration) (mBART model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [FlaxRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.FlaxRobertaForMaskedLM) (RoBERTa model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, FlaxAutoModelForMaskedLM
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForMaskedLM.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a masked language modeling head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [FlaxAlbertForMaskedLM](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.FlaxAlbertForMaskedLM) (ALBERT model)
- **bart** -- [FlaxBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.FlaxBartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
- **bert** -- [FlaxBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.FlaxBertForMaskedLM) (BERT model)
- **big_bird** -- [FlaxBigBirdForMaskedLM](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.FlaxBigBirdForMaskedLM) (BigBird model)
- **distilbert** -- [FlaxDistilBertForMaskedLM](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.FlaxDistilBertForMaskedLM) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [FlaxElectraForMaskedLM](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.FlaxElectraForMaskedLM) (ELECTRA model)
- **mbart** -- [FlaxMBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.FlaxMBartForConditionalGeneration) (mBART model)
- **roberta** -- [FlaxRobertaForMaskedLM](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.FlaxRobertaForMaskedLM) (RoBERTa model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _PyTorch state_dict save file_ (e.g, `./pt_model/pytorch_model.bin`). In
    this case, `from_pt` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the PyTorch model in a
    TensorFlow model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the TensorFlow model
    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, FlaxAutoModelForMaskedLM

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForMaskedLM.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForMaskedLM.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pt_model_config.json')
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForMaskedLM.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pytorch_model.bin', from_pt=True, config=config)
```


## FlaxAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM

<a id='transformers.FlaxAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM'></a>
> **class transformers.FlaxAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence-to-sequence language modeling head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence-to-sequence language modeling head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.FlaxBartForConditionalGeneration) (BART model)
  - [EncoderDecoderConfig](model_doc/encoderdecoder.html#transformers.EncoderDecoderConfig) configuration class: [FlaxEncoderDecoderModel](model_doc/encoderdecoder.html#transformers.FlaxEncoderDecoderModel) (Encoder decoder model)
  - [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) configuration class: [FlaxMBartForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.FlaxMBartForConditionalGeneration) (mBART model)
  - [MT5Config](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.MT5Config) configuration class: [FlaxMT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/mt5.html#transformers.FlaxMT5ForConditionalGeneration) (mT5 model)
  - [MarianConfig](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.MarianConfig) configuration class: [FlaxMarianMTModel](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.FlaxMarianMTModel) (Marian model)
  - [PegasusConfig](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.PegasusConfig) configuration class: [FlaxPegasusForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/pegasus.html#transformers.FlaxPegasusForConditionalGeneration) (Pegasus model)
  - [T5Config](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.T5Config) configuration class: [FlaxT5ForConditionalGeneration](model_doc/t5.html#transformers.FlaxT5ForConditionalGeneration) (T5 model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, FlaxAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('t5-base')
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForSeq2SeqLM.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence-to-sequence language modeling head) from a pretrained model.

- **marian** -- [FlaxMarianMTModel](model_doc/marian.html#transformers.FlaxMarianMTModel) (Marian model)



## FlaxAutoModelForSequenceClassification

<a id='transformers.FlaxAutoModelForSequenceClassification'></a>
> **class transformers.FlaxAutoModelForSequenceClassification**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence classification head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>

Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence classification head) from a configuration.

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxAlbertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.FlaxAlbertForSequenceClassification) (ALBERT model)
  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBartForSequenceClassification](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.FlaxBartForSequenceClassification) (BART model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBertForSequenceClassification](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.FlaxBertForSequenceClassification) (BERT model)

<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a sequence classification head) from a pretrained model.

  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, FlaxAutoModelForSequenceClassification

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pt_model_config.json')
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForSequenceClassification.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pytorch_model.bin', from_pt=True, config=config)
```


## FlaxAutoModelForQuestionAnswering

<a id='transformers.FlaxAutoModelForQuestionAnswering'></a>
> **class transformers.FlaxAutoModelForQuestionAnswering**(*args, **kwargs)


This is a generic model class that will be instantiated as one of the model classes of the library (with a question answering head) when created
with the `from_pretrained()` class method or the
`from_config()` class method.

This class cannot be instantiated directly using `__init__()` (throws an error).


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_config'></a>
> **from\_config**(**kwargs)


Instantiates one of the model classes of the library (with a question answering head) from a configuration.

Note:
Loading a model from its configuration file does **not** load the model weights. It only affects the
model's configuration. Use `from_pretrained()` to load the model
weights.

> Parameters

- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig)) --
  The model class to instantiate is selected based on the configuration class:

  - [AlbertConfig](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.AlbertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxAlbertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.FlaxAlbertForQuestionAnswering) (ALBERT model)
  - [BartConfig](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.BartConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBartForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.FlaxBartForQuestionAnswering) (BART model)
  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.FlaxBertForQuestionAnswering) (BERT model)
  - [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBigBirdForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.FlaxBigBirdForQuestionAnswering) (BigBird model)
  - [DistilBertConfig](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.DistilBertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxDistilBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.FlaxDistilBertForQuestionAnswering) (DistilBERT model)
  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [FlaxElectraForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.FlaxElectraForQuestionAnswering) (ELECTRA model)
  - [MBartConfig](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.MBartConfig) configuration class: [FlaxMBartForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.FlaxMBartForQuestionAnswering) (mBART model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [FlaxRobertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.FlaxRobertaForQuestionAnswering) (RoBERTa model)

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, FlaxAutoModelForQuestionAnswering
>>> # Download configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForQuestionAnswering.from_config(config)
```


<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
> **from\_pretrained**(*model_args, **kwargs)


Instantiate one of the model classes of the library (with a question answering head) from a pretrained model.

The model class to instantiate is selected based on the `model_type` property of the config object (either
passed as an argument or loaded from `pretrained_model_name_or_path` if possible), or when it's missing,
by falling back to using pattern matching on `pretrained_model_name_or_path`:

- **albert** -- [FlaxAlbertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/albert.html#transformers.FlaxAlbertForQuestionAnswering) (ALBERT model)
- **bart** -- [FlaxBartForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bart.html#transformers.FlaxBartForQuestionAnswering) (BART model)
- **bert** -- [FlaxBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.FlaxBertForQuestionAnswering) (BERT model)
- **big_bird** -- [FlaxBigBirdForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.FlaxBigBirdForQuestionAnswering) (BigBird model)
- **distilbert** -- [FlaxDistilBertForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/distilbert.html#transformers.FlaxDistilBertForQuestionAnswering) (DistilBERT model)
- **electra** -- [FlaxElectraForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.FlaxElectraForQuestionAnswering) (ELECTRA model)
- **mbart** -- [FlaxMBartForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/mbart.html#transformers.FlaxMBartForQuestionAnswering) (mBART model)
- **roberta** -- [FlaxRobertaForQuestionAnswering](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.FlaxRobertaForQuestionAnswering) (RoBERTa model)

> Parameters

- **pretrained_model_name_or_path** (`str` or `os.PathLike`) --
  Can be either:

  - A string, the _model id_ of a pretrained model hosted inside a model repo on huggingface.co.
    Valid model ids can be located at the root-level, like `bert-base-uncased`, or namespaced under
    a user or organization name, like `dbmdz/bert-base-german-cased`.
  - A path to a _directory_ containing model weights saved using
    [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained), e.g., `./my_model_directory/`.
  - A path or url to a _PyTorch state_dict save file_ (e.g, `./pt_model/pytorch_model.bin`). In
    this case, `from_pt` should be set to `True` and a configuration object should be provided
    as `config` argument. This loading path is slower than converting the PyTorch model in a
    TensorFlow model using the provided conversion scripts and loading the TensorFlow model
    afterwards.
- **model_args** (additional positional arguments, _optional_) --
  Will be passed along to the underlying model `__init__()` method.
- **config** ([PretrainedConfig](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig), _optional_) --
  Configuration for the model to use instead of an automatically loaded configuration. Configuration can
  be automatically loaded when:

  - The model is a model provided by the library (loaded with the _model id_ string of a pretrained
    model).
  - The model was saved using [save_pretrained()](main_classes/model.html#transformers.PreTrainedModel.save_pretrained) and is reloaded
    by supplying the save directory.
  - The model is loaded by supplying a local directory as `pretrained_model_name_or_path` and a
    configuration JSON file named _config.json_ is found in the directory.
- **cache_dir** (`str` or `os.PathLike`, _optional_) --
  Path to a directory in which a downloaded pretrained model configuration should be cached if the
  standard cache should not be used.
- **from_pt** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Load the model weights from a PyTorch checkpoint save file (see docstring of
  `pretrained_model_name_or_path` argument).
- **force_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to force the (re-)download of the model weights and configuration files, overriding the
  cached versions if they exist.
- **resume_download** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to delete incompletely received files. Will attempt to resume the download if such a
  file exists.
- **proxies** (`Dict[str, str]`, _optional_) --
  A dictionary of proxy servers to use by protocol or endpoint, e.g., `&lcub'http': 'foo.bar:3128', 'http://hostname': 'foo.bar:4012'}`. The proxies are used on each request.
- **output_loading_info(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether ot not to also return a dictionary containing missing keys, unexpected keys and error messages.
- **local_files_only(`bool`,** _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to only look at local files (e.g., not try downloading the model).
- **revision(`str`,** _optional_, defaults to `"main"`) --
  The specific model version to use. It can be a branch name, a tag name, or a commit id, since we use a
  git-based system for storing models and other artifacts on huggingface.co, so `revision` can be any
  identifier allowed by git.
- **trust_remote_code** (`bool`, _optional_, defaults to `False`) --
  Whether or not to allow for custom models defined on the Hub in their own modeling files. This option
  should only be set to `True` for repositories you trust and in which you have read the code, as it
  will execute code present on the Hub on your local machine.
- **kwargs** (additional keyword arguments, _optional_) --
  Can be used to update the configuration object (after it being loaded) and initiate the model (e.g.,
  `output_attentions=True`). Behaves differently depending on whether a `config` is provided or
  automatically loaded:

  - If a configuration is provided with `config`, `**kwargs` will be directly passed to the
    underlying model's `__init__` method (we assume all relevant updates to the configuration have
    already been done)
  - If a configuration is not provided, `kwargs` will be first passed to the configuration class
    initialization function ([from_pretrained()](main_classes/configuration.html#transformers.PretrainedConfig.from_pretrained)). Each key of
    `kwargs` that corresponds to a configuration attribute will be used to override said attribute
    with the supplied `kwargs` value. Remaining keys that do not correspond to any configuration
    attribute will be passed to the underlying model's `__init__` function.

> Examples:

```python
>>> from transformers import AutoConfig, FlaxAutoModelForQuestionAnswering

>>> # Download model and configuration from huggingface.co and cache.
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForQuestionAnswering.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased')

>>> # Update configuration during loading
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForQuestionAnswering.from_pretrained('bert-base-cased', output_attentions=True)
>>> model.config.output_attentions
True

>>> # Loading from a PyTorch checkpoint file instead of a TensorFlow model (slower)
>>> config = AutoConfig.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pt_model_config.json')
>>> model = FlaxAutoModelForQuestionAnswering.from_pretrained('./pt_model/bert_pytorch_model.bin', from_pt=True, config=config)
```

`from_config()` class method.

  - [BertConfig](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.BertConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBertForTokenClassification](model_doc/bert.html#transformers.FlaxBertForTokenClassification) (BERT model)
  - [BigBirdConfig](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.BigBirdConfig) configuration class: [FlaxBigBirdForTokenClassification](model_doc/bigbird.html#transformers.FlaxBigBirdForTokenClassification) (BigBird model)

  - [ElectraConfig](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.ElectraConfig) configuration class: [FlaxElectraForTokenClassification](model_doc/electra.html#transformers.FlaxElectraForTokenClassification) (ELECTRA model)
  - [RobertaConfig](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.RobertaConfig) configuration class: [FlaxRobertaForTokenClassification](model_doc/roberta.html#transformers.FlaxRobertaForTokenClassification) (RoBERTa model)



<a id='transformers.models.auto.auto_factory._BaseAutoModelClass.from_pretrained'></a>
